The leeward wall's height changes the SHAPE only, not the load values ŌĆö matching the 1-story. Prior rev ŌĆö rev 43 ŌĆö **MIXED-HEIGHT TWO-STORY ŌĆö SECTION CUT DIAPHRAGMS NOW CONNECT TO EACH WALL'S TOP + DEFORM ON HEIGHT EDIT (like the 1-story).** The user asked to bring two behaviors of the original 1-story `SecDiagram` into the mixed `SecDiagramSeq`: (1) editing a wall's pressure/height updates the Level 1 / Level 2 diaphragm values, and (2) the nodes are connected so changing a wall height makes the shape DEFORM (the 1-story draws a sloping ROOF LINE between the two wall tops). Root issue with (2): the mixed section drew each diaphragm as a FLAT horizontal line pinned at the MAX wall height (`yF2`/`yRoof`) with each wall an independent vertical, so changing a non-tallest wall's height left a gap and nothing visibly connected ŌĆö and that flat-pinned look also made height edits read as "nothing updates." Fix (display/UI only ŌĆö guarded engine byte-identical): the Level-1 (floor) diaphragm is now a **polyline through every wall's own 1st-story top** (`floorY(i)=wallBotŌłÆH┬ĘpxPerFt`) with a NODE at each, and the Level-2 (roof) diaphragm is a **polyline through the 2-story block walls' full tops** (`roofY(i)=wallBotŌłÆ(H+HŌéé)┬ĘpxPerFt`) with nodes ŌĆö exactly the 1-story's sloping roof line generalized to N walls. Change any wall's H/HŌéé and its node moves, so the diaphragm slopes/steps and the section deforms as one CONNECTED shape; when all heights match the polylines collapse to flat lines (a uniform building looks identical to before ŌĆö no regression). The value callouts ("Level 1/Level 2 ŌĆ” plf") now anchor to the diaphragm's leeward END (`cFloorY`/`cRoofY`) so they ride the slope; the redundant parapet-start node moved to the parapet TOP so it no longer double-draws over a diaphragm node. For (1): the values were already recomputed live from `section.seq`/`v` (which App recomputes from `wallProps` on every edit) ŌĆö confirmed by test ŌĆö so editing a block wall's HŌéé/pw raises Level 1 (the poured-forward ┬Į┬ĘHŌéé┬Ępw) AND Level 2 (the block's ┬Į┬ĘHŌéé┬Ępw), and parapet edits raise the parapet terms; the deficiency the user saw was the flat shape, now fixed. **Engine guard CLEAN (12/12 byte-identical); compile clean; render smoke PASS (modular ŌēĪ inlined preview); rev-41 + rev-42 regressions still 8/8; NEW `_rev43_connect.cjs` PASSES 10/10** (floor diaphragm is a 4-pt polyline that slopes to a short leeward wall; roof is a 2-pt polyline that slopes when block HŌéé differ; Ōēź6 connection nodes; uniform heights ŌåÆ FLAT floor line; Level-2 value 404ŌåÆ484 when block HŌéé 10ŌåÆ20; ŌåÆ474 when block pw 16ŌåÆ30). `APP_BUILD = 123` ("Version 1.23"). The floating input branches: `edit.key` ŌåÆ reads `ebuf ?? seqVal` and writes `commit(key,prop,num)`; else ŌåÆ the existing `v`/`upd` front-back path. Values stay LIVE with no extra wiring: edits write to `wallProps[key]`, so `propsFor` ŌåÆ `activeSection.seq` recompute every render, and `roofLLseq`/`seqAcc`/the diagram already read from `seq` ŌĆö so a block-wall height/pressure edit flows straight into the Level-2 value, the Level-1 accumulation, and the drawn arrows. Prior rev ŌĆö rev 34 ŌĆö **FLOOR DIAPHRAGM NO LONGER DOUBLE-COUNTS THE ROOF LOAD (2-story section-cut + plan display fix; user-requested).** In 2-story mode the 2nd-floor (level-2) diaphragm line load was being shown as ┬Į┬ĘH┬Ępw + ┬Į┬ĘHŌéé┬Ępw + **roof diaphragm** (e.g. 104+104+374 = **582 plf**). That double-counts the roof: the correct load path is roof diaphragm ŌåÆ 2nd-story shear wall ŌåÆ (as a POINT load) 1st-story shear wall, so the floor diaphragm itself carries ONLY the half-walls directly above and below it. The displayed 2nd-floor diaphragm load now drops to the FLOOR-ONLY ┬Į┬ĘH┬Ępw + ┬Į┬ĘHŌéé┬Ępw (104+104 = **208 plf**). Three DISPLAY-ONLY spots changed: (1) the section-cut window (`floorLL = wallRes + wallRes2`, dropped `+ roofLL`; removed the "roof load transferred Ōåō" breakdown row ŌĆö the big number AND the `SecDiagram2` gold callout both follow `floorLL`); (2) the on-plan line-load LABEL when viewing the **1st floor** (new `floorDiaphragmPlf(key) = 0.5┬Ępw┬Ę(H+HŌéé)`, passed to `WindLoad` as a new `displayPlf` prop ŌĆö uniform along the wall, so it collapses to ONE label); (3) the within-wall dashed tributary divides are hidden on the 1st floor (the floor load no longer varies along a wall there; the leeward-parapet variation that created them lives only in the ROOF diaphragm). **CRUCIALLY the REACTIONS / on-plan POINT LOADS, base shear, and stacked overturning/holdown are UNCHANGED** ŌĆö `propsForActive` (1st floor still `H_eff = H + 2┬ĘHŌéé`), `buildSecData`/`lineReactions`, `secH`/`secV`, `runDesignHandoff`/`forceLbs`, and the status-bar base shear all still use the COMBINED load, so the 11.35k point loads and the Design-tab stacking are byte-identical. By construction 208 + roof-via-wall reaction ŌēĪ the old 582 single-load reaction, so only the *label* moved, not the statics. **NO guarded engine fn touched** (`buildSecData`/`lineReactions`/`findLeewardPartner` untouched; the change lives in `WindWindow` display vars, the presentational `WindLoad`, the new `floorDiaphragmPlf` helper, and the plan render JSX). esbuild compile clean (only the pre-existing duplicate-key warnings in the unused `Elevation`). `APP_BUILD = 114` ("Version 1.14"). > **rev 44 ŌĆö MIXED-HEIGHT TWO-STORY ┬Ę LEEWARD-MOST WALL HEIGHT EDITABLE (geometry-only) + DEFAULT WALL HEIGHT 10ft (user-requested).** Two fixes. (1) The user noted that the 1-story section cut lets you edit the leeward wall's height (for correct geometry) even though that wall has no load, and asked for the same on the mixed section cut's LAST wall in the wind direction. (2) Make the default wall height 10ft and parapet 5ft.
> - **Leeward-most wall height editable.** `SecDiagramSeq`'s back-box group previously rendered only when the back wall had a parapet (`w.par>0`) and exposed only `qLee` + parapet height ŌĆö the wall's HEIGHT was fixed. It now ALWAYS renders an `H` box (`field="leeH" prop="leeH"` ŌåÆ `upd` ŌåÆ `setVals("lee",{H})`) and, when the back wall is 2-story (Section C), an `HŌéé` box (`leeH2` ŌåÆ `setVals("lee",{H2})`); the parapet pressure/height boxes stay gated on `par>0`. `propOf(last)` already read `v.leeH`/`v.leeH2`, and the open-section seed already populates them from the leeward partner ŌĆö so editing the box flows into the rev-43 connected diaphragm polyline and the leeward wall redraws/deforms (its top node moves), exactly like the 1-story's editable `HR` tilting the roof line. The leeward wall carries no diaphragm load, so this is geometry-only: it routes through `upd`/`"lee"` (NOT the interior `commit` path) and does NOT change the Level-1/Level-2 load values ŌĆö same as the 1-story, where `wallRes` uses the windward `HL` and `HR` only sets the roof slope.
> - **Default wall height 10ft.** `DEF_SECTION.H: 13 ŌåÆ 10` (parapet already 5; HŌéé is null ŌåÆ equals H, so a new wall is H=10, HŌéé=10, par=5). VALUE-only change ŌĆö no schema field renamed/added/removed, so the load-state schema tripwire (locks field NAMES) is unaffected; re-run `test_schema.cjs` to confirm and, only if it also snapshots default values, update `schema.expected.json` (intentional change). > **rev 43 ŌĆö MIXED-HEIGHT TWO-STORY ┬Ę SECTION-CUT DIAPHRAGMS CONNECT TO EACH WALL'S TOP + DEFORM ON HEIGHT EDIT (user-requested; ports two 1-story behaviors).** The user asked to make the mixed section cut (`SecDiagramSeq`) behave like the original 1-story `SecDiagram` in two ways: (1) changing a wall's pressure/height updates the Level 1 / Level 2 diaphragm values; (2) the nodes are connected so changing a wall height deforms the shape (the 1-story draws a sloping ROOF LINE polygon between the windward + leeward wall tops, with node circles that reposition live). Study of `SecDiagram`: it reads all geometry from the live `v` buffer (`roofYL=wallBotŌłÆHL┬ĘpxPerFt`, `roofYR=wallBotŌłÆHR┬ĘpxPerFt`), draws the wall as a trapezoid whose top edge is the roof line, and the line load value reads `v` too ŌĆö so both behaviors fall out of "draw from the live values + connect the tops."
> - **Root cause (2).** `SecDiagramSeq` drew the floor diaphragm as ONE flat `<line>` at `yF2 = wallBot ŌłÆ max(H)┬ĘpxPerFt` and the roof diaphragm as one flat `<line>` at `yRoof = wallBot ŌłÆ max(H+HŌéé)┬ĘpxPerFt`, with each wall an independent vertical. So a non-tallest wall's top sat BELOW the flat diaphragm (a gap) and editing its height moved only that stub ŌĆö nothing "connected," and the pinned-flat look made height edits read as inert.
> - **Fix.** New per-wall levels `floorY(i)=wallBotŌłÆW[i].H┬ĘpxPerFt` (1st-story top) and `roofY(i)=wallBotŌłÆ(W[i].H+(one?0:HŌéé))┬ĘpxPerFt` (full top). The Level-1 diaphragm is now `<polyline>` through `floorY(i)` for ALL walls + a node `<circle>` at each; the Level-2 diaphragm is a `<polyline>` through `roofY(i)` over the block (`twoIdx`) + nodes. Each wall's top coincides with its diaphragm node, so they connect; change any H/HŌéé and the node moves ŌåÆ the diaphragm slopes/steps ŌåÆ the section deforms as one connected shape (the 1-story sloping roof, generalized to N walls). When all heights match, the polylines are flat == the old look (uniform building unchanged). The value callouts anchor to the diaphragm's leeward end (`cFloorY=floorY(last)`, `cRoofY=roofY(block last)`) so they ride the slope; the parapet-start node moved to the parapet TOP (`pty`) so it doesn't double-draw over a diaphragm node.
> - **Behaviour (1) ŌĆö already live, now confirmed + visible.** `WindWindow` computes `floorLLmix`/`roofLLseq` from `section.seq` and `v` in its render body, and `activeSection.seq` is recomputed from `propsFor` (=`wallProps`) every App render ŌĆö so a block-wall edit (interior `commit` ŌåÆ `wallProps`) or a front/back edit (`v`/`upd`, which also writes `wallProps`) flows straight into the values. Editing a block wall's HŌéé/pw raises Level 1 (the poured-forward ┬Į┬ĘHŌéé┬Ępw `seqAcc`) AND Level 2 (the block's ┬Į┬ĘHŌéé┬Ępw); parapet edits raise the parapet terms. The leeward wall's HEIGHT changes only the SHAPE (now visibly, via the polyline) and not the load value ŌĆö exactly like the 1-story, where the leeward `HR` tilts the roof line but `wallRes` uses the windward `HL`.

> **rev 42 ŌĆö MIXED-HEIGHT TWO-STORY ┬Ę INTERIOR BLOCK WALLS NOW FULLY EDITABLE ŌĆö height + pressure (user-requested).** The user asked to remove the rev-41 limitation: the 2-story BLOCK walls drawn in the middle of the mixed section cut (`SecDiagramSeq`) were display-only, so their height/pressure couldn't be changed ŌĆö "the walls need to be as editable as the rest of the walls." The block FRONT wall (windward face, drawn only when `bw!==0`) gets `pw` ┬Ę `H` ┬Ę `HŌéé` ┬Ę `par` ┬Ę `qWind`; the block BACK wall (leeward face, `bl!==last`) gets `qLee` ┬Ę `par` ┬Ę `H` ┬Ę `HŌéé` ŌĆö the same set the front/back already expose. The gates `bw!==0`/`bl!==last` ensure a block end that IS the sequence front/back keeps its original front/back boxes (no double box). The floating input branches on `edit.key`: keyed ŌåÆ value `= ebuf["key:prop"] ?? String(seqVal(key,prop))`, `onChange` writes `ebuf` + `commit(key,prop,num(raw))`, `onBlur` clears that `ebuf` entry; unkeyed ŌåÆ the existing `v`/`upd` path. Enter/Escape now blur (so the keyed path's buffer cleanup runs).
> - **Why values stay live with no extra wiring.** A keyed edit writes `wallProps[key]`; `propsFor` is derived from `wallProps`, and `activeSection.seq` (hence `section.seq` in `WindWindow`) recomputes from `propsFor` on every render. `roofLLseq`, the floor accumulation `seqAcc`, and `SecDiagramSeq`'s own `propOf(interior)` all already read from `seq` ŌĆö so editing a block wall's `HŌéé`/`pw`/parapet flows straight into the Level-2 diaphragm value, the Level-1 accumulation, and the drawn arrows, exactly like a front/back edit. (Front/back edits go through `v` and also write `wallProps`, so the two paths stay consistent.)

> **rev 40 ŌĆö MIXED-HEIGHT TWO-STORY ┬Ę SEQUENCE-BASED OVERALL SECTION CUT (A/B/C/C-reverse).** The user flagged two things on the rev-39 section cut: it changed between the 1st- and 2nd-floor plans (it should be ONE overall-building section), and Section C rendered like Section A. Root causes: (a) the open-section `useEffect` resolved the windward wall from the floor-filtered `secH/secV`, so on the 2nd floor the 1-story windward wall was missing and a different wall anchored the section; (b) `SecDiagramMix` only ever drew "1-story front + one 2-story block + 1-story back", so any cut ending on a 2-story wall (Section C) still drew a closing 1-story wall (Section A). Both fixed by switching to a SEQUENCE model:
> - **`sectionSequence(sAcross, axis, sign, graph, propsFor, isOne)`** (module fn, after `nearestTwoStoryBehind`) ŌĆö returns the ordered list of every across-wind (`recv`) wall whose span includes the cut's across-wind position `sAcross`, sorted by downwind depth (windwardŌåÆleeward), each `{key, one, H, H2, par, pw, qWind, qLee, depth}`. Always the FULL graph ŌåÆ floor-independent. The 1/2-story pattern IS the section type: `1┬Ę2┬Ę2┬Ę1`=A, `1┬Ę1`=B, `1┬Ę2┬Ę2`=C, `2┬Ę2┬Ę1`=C-reverse.
> - **Floor independence** ŌĆö the open-section `useEffect` now computes `seq = sectionSequence(po.sAcross, ŌĆ”full graphŌĆ”)` and sets `activeWall.key = seq[0].key` (the true windward wall) instead of falling back to the filtered `sc.windLoads[0]`. So the SAME wall anchors the section on either floor. `activeSection` also carries `seq` (recomputed from `activeWall.sAcross`, or the wall's center as a fallback).
> - **`SecDiagramSeq({seq,v,upd,floorLL})`** REPLACES `SecDiagramMix`. Draws N walls evenly spaced frontŌåÆback, each at its own height (1-story green to `H`+parapet, 2-story dark to `H+HŌéé`+parapet); the floor diaphragm dashes across ALL walls at the 1-story top, the roof diaphragm spans the contiguous 2-story block (`twoIdx`); windward pressure on the front wall (full height+parapet), leeward pressure on the back; front & back walls editable via the live `v`/`upd` buffer (incl. an HŌéé box when the front wall is 2-story, for C-reverse), interior walls display-only. Handles all 4 types from the sequence alone ŌĆö no per-type branching.
> - **`WindWindow`** ŌĆö `seq = section.seq||[]`; `hasOne/hasTwo`; `mixedSeq = twoStory && hasOne && hasTwo && seq.length>=2`. Diagram: `mixedSeq ? <SecDiagramSeq> : twoStoryView ? <SecDiagram2> : <SecDiagram>`. The floor-diaphragm line load = `seqBase + seqLeePar + seqAcc` where `seqBase = ┬Į┬ĘH┬Ępw + (front 1-story ? windPar : 0)`, `seqAcc = front 1-story ? ┬Į┬ĘHŌéé┬Ępw of the nearest 2-story in the sequence : ┬Į┬ĘHŌéé┬Ępw of the front wall itself`, `seqLeePar` counted only if the BACK wall is 1-story ŌĆö matching `buildSecDataF1`. Breakdown panel shows ┬Į┬ĘH┬Ępw + parapets + the poured-forward ┬Į┬ĘHŌéé┬Ępw (= 478 in the user's HŌéé=13 case). Section B (all 1-story) ŌåÆ `SecDiagram`; uniform 2-story ŌåÆ `SecDiagram2`; both unchanged.

> **rev 39 ŌĆö MIXED-HEIGHT TWO-STORY ┬Ę STEPPED SECTION CUT (user follow-up to Step 4).** The user noted the Step-4 section cut "doesn't look like the schematics": a 1-story cut drew a flat single-story elevation, but the schematic SECTION A (the 454) is a *stepped* section ŌĆö the 1-story windward wall AND the 2-story block standing behind it (the source of the +80). This rev adds it. **`nearestTwoStoryBehind(key, axis, sign, graph, propsFor, isOne)`** (module fn) mirrors `buildSecDataF1`'s `backs` scan to find the nearest 2-story `recv`-orientation wall downwind of the windward wall, returning its props (or null). `activeSection.behind` is set to that (only when the cut wall `isOneStory`). A 1-story wall with nothing 2-story behind ŌåÆ still the plain single-story window; pure 2-story cuts ŌåÆ `SecDiagram2` unchanged; `SecDiagram`/`SecDiagram2` and the guarded engine untouched. **Verification:** engine guard CLEAN (12/12), compile clean, render smoke PASS (32,149), Steps 2/3/4 regressions PASS, NEW `work/test_step4b.cjs` PASSES (`nearestTwoStoryBehind` returns the box with HŌéé=10 behind the windward perimeter wall; `WindWindow` SSR routes a 1-story+behind cut to the stepped diagram showing the "2-STORY"/"BEHIND" block + the "2-story portion behind" breakdown term + "Floor diaphragm line load", and NOT the 2-story roof/floor split; a 1-story+nothing-behind cut shows the plain "Total wall line load"). `APP_BUILD = 119` ("Version 1.19"). **The stepped diagram is a first cut built to match SECTION A from the schematic ŌĆö its exact proportions/labels are pending the user's eyeball in the preview and are easy to tune (it's one self-contained component).** Deploy: replace `src/plan-sketcher-suite.jsx` ONLY ŌĆö `calcCore.js` UNCHANGED. > **rev 37 ŌĆö MIXED-HEIGHT TWO-STORY ┬Ę STEP 3/4: 1ST-FLOOR (FLOOR DIAPHRAGM) ACCUMULATION ŌĆö "THE 454".** On the 1st-floor view + floor-1 design of a building with Ōēź1 tagged 1-story wall, a windward wall's floor-diaphragm plf VARIES along its length: each across-wind sub-region sums the strips connected to the FLOOR diaphragm in its downwind shadow, so the front wall splits into regions (the user's worked example: `32├Ś5 + 16├Ś13/2 + 22├Ś5 = 374` where nothing two-story is behind it, `+ 16├Ś10/2 = 454` where the box is). Matches the "1ST FLOOR PLAN" schematic; the dashed tributary divide is drawn at each 454/374 boundary. **New additive fn `buildSecDataF1(section, graph, loop, isSup, propsFor, isOne)`** ŌĆö a focused copy of `buildSecData` (same windward + overlap-shadow + line-grouping + back-wall-subdivision machinery; reuses `findLeewardPartner` and `lineReactions` verbatim) with the floor-1 mixed load rule swapped in. Per windward wall the sub-region plf = `base + leePar┬ĘqLee + acc` where: `base` = ┬Į┬ĘH┬Ępw + (1-story ? own parapet┬ĘqWind : ┬Į┬ĘHŌéé┬Ępw of its own upper wall); `leePar` = the exterior (farthest-downwind) back wall's parapet but ONLY if that back wall is 1-story (a 2-story back wall's parapet belongs to the roof diaphragm); `acc` = ┬Į┬ĘHŌéé┬Ępw of the NEAREST 2-story back wall covering the sub-region (ONE face ŌĆö the bottom half of its upper wall; its top half already went to the roof). Back walls are gathered exactly like `buildSecData`'s `backs` (downwind, `recv` orientation, overlapping across-wind), now tagged with `{par (if 1-story), h2 (if 2-story), d}`; breakpoints at their lo/hi split the windward span ŌåÆ the 454/374 regions. **Wiring:** `mixed1 = twoStory && activeFloor===1 && oneStory.size>0`; the live `secH`/`secV` call `buildSecDataF1(sections.*, graph, loop, isSup, propsFor /*RAW, not propsForActive*/, isOneStory)` when `mixed1`, else `buildSecData` as before; `buildFloor(1)` does the same via a local `mixedF1`. The rev-34 `displayPlf` override (`floorDiaphragmPlf`) and the `divides` hide are both re-gated `ŌĆ”&&!mixed1`, so the mixed wall shows its true per-region 454/374 labels + divides, while a uniform 2-story building (no tags) is byte-identical to rev 36. **Why a sibling fn, not an edit:** the floor-1 mixed model differs structurally (the front wall accumulates a deeper wall's load, and parapets route by wall type) ŌĆö and the guarded `buildSecData` must stay byte-identical; a copy keeps both. **Verification:** engine guard CLEAN (12/12), esbuild compile clean, SSR render smoke PASS (32,149), Step-2 regression PASS, and new checked-in **`work/test_step3.cjs`** runs the REAL bundled `buildSecDataF1` on a 1-story-perimeter + 2-story-box fixture and asserts the windward wall's sub-regions are exactly `[374,374,454]`, `╬ö = ┬Į┬ĘHŌéé┬Ępw = 80`, the **middle third over the box carries 454**, the box walls are NOT separately loaded (shadowed ŌåÆ accumulated forward), and a divide is emitted. `APP_BUILD = 117` ("Version 1.17"). Deploy: replace `src/plan-sketcher-suite.jsx` ONLY ŌĆö `calcCore.js` UNCHANGED. See ┬¦4ll. Remaining: Step 4 (section cuts + handoff finalize).

> **rev 36 ŌĆö MIXED-HEIGHT TWO-STORY ┬Ę STEP 2/4: 2ND-FLOOR (ROOF DIAPHRAGM) EXCLUDES 1-STORY WALLS.** The tag now changes behavior. On the **2nd-floor** plan + design, a 1-story (green) wall no longer exists for the roof diaphragm: it collects no line load, casts no overlap-shadow, and takes no point-load reaction ŌĆö only the two-story walls carry the roof and form its lateral system (matches the user's "2nd floor plan" schematic; the live metrics' base shear drops accordingly). The **1st-floor** view and **1-story mode** are untouched (Step 3 handles floor 1). **Implementation ŌĆö the guarded engine is byte-identical; it simply receives a filtered graph:** new memo `twoStoryGraph` = `{edges: graph.edges.filter(e=>!oneStory.has(keyOf(e))), nodes: graph.nodes that those edges still use}` (empty `oneStory` or 1-story mode ŌåÆ returns `graph` itself, so untagged buildings are unchanged); new memo `twoStoryLoop = loopInfo(twoStoryGraph.nodes, twoStoryGraph.edges)` (the box closes into its own ring ŌåÆ exact exterior normals, even though the full perimeter+box graph has `loop===null`). The render path picks `secGraph/secLoop = (twoStory&&activeFloor===2) ? twoStoryGraph/twoStoryLoop : graph/loop` and feeds them to the existing `buildSecData`; `secH`/`secV` deps updated. The design handoff's `buildFloor(floor)` gained `fg/fl` locals (= filtered graph/loop when `twoStory&&floor===2`) used for its `buildSecData` calls, the reaction-edge lookup, and the support-extent scan; `runDesignHandoff` deps gained `twoStoryGraph`/`twoStoryLoop`. **Why graph-filtering, not prop-zeroing:** the engine's `overlapShadow` test would let a 1-story wall sitting in FRONT of the box wrongly shadow (drop) the box's windward wall; removing the wall from the graph entirely is the clean fix and needs no engine edit. **Walls still all RENDER** off the full `graph` (green 1-story walls are drawn, just load-less on floor 2). > **rev 35 ŌĆö MIXED-HEIGHT TWO-STORY ┬Ę STEP 1/4: ONE-STORY WALL TAGGING (user-requested, multi-step in progress).** Goal of the whole feature: model buildings that are two-story overall but where some walls/portions are only one story (single-story or open-to-above) ŌĆö e.g. a 2-story box inside a 1-story perimeter (see the user's schematics). A one-story wall is a diaphragm-connectivity statement: it touches the **floor** diaphragm (its parapet + top-half + own roof at the floor level) and the **foundation**, but never the **roof** diaphragm. **Step 1 is the tag + appearance ONLY** ŌĆö zero load/analysis change, so a building with no tags is byte-identical to rev 34. > **rev 34 ŌĆö FLOOR DIAPHRAGM STOPS DOUBLE-COUNTING THE ROOF LOAD (display fix, user-requested).** The 2-story load-path display was wrong: the 2nd-floor diaphragm line load was rendered as `wallRes + wallRes2 + roofLL` (┬Į┬ĘH┬Ępw + ┬Į┬ĘHŌéé┬Ępw + the whole roof diaphragm incl. parapets) ŌĆö i.e. it poured the roof load into the floor diaphragm. Physically the roof diaphragm dumps into the 2nd-story shear wall, which transfers down into the 1st-story shear wall as a POINT load; the floor diaphragm only spans the half-walls above/below it. So the displayed floor diaphragm is now FLOOR-ONLY: `floorLL = wallRes + wallRes2` (= ┬Į┬ĘH┬Ępw + ┬Į┬ĘHŌéé┬Ępw; 104+104 = **208 plf** for the H=HŌéé=13, pw=16 example, vs the old 582). **Edits (all DISPLAY-only, all outside the guarded engine):** (1) `WindWindow`: `floorLL` formula drops `+ roofLL`, and the "roof load transferred Ōåō" breakdown `<div>` is removed; the section-cut big number and the `SecDiagram2` gold "2nd-flr diaphragm" callout both read `floorLL`, so both update. (2) New `floorDiaphragmPlf = useCallback(key => 0.5┬Ępw┬Ę(H+HŌéé))` next to `propsForActive`, using the REAL (un-substituted) `propsFor` H/HŌéé. The leeward-parapet term cancels (it's only in the roof), so the floor value is uniform along a wall. (3) `WindLoad` gains a `displayPlf` prop: when non-null it renders ONE span (waŌåÆwb) at that plf instead of the per-region coalesced subLoads; passed only when `twoStory && activeFloor===1`. (4) The dashed tributary `divides` render is gated off when `twoStory && activeFloor===1` (uniform floor load ŌåÆ no within-wall divide). **UNCHANGED on purpose (the point loads must keep stacking):** `propsForActive` (1st floor stays `H_eff = H + 2┬ĘHŌéé`), `buildSecData`, `lineReactions`, `findLeewardPartner`, `secH`/`secV`, `runDesignHandoff`/`forceLbs`, base shear, and all Design-tab stacking. The reaction off 208 plf + the level-2 wall reaction transferred down equals the old single 582-plf reaction by construction, so the on-plan point loads (11.35k in the user's case) and holdown stacking are byte-identical ŌĆö only the line-load LABEL changed. So at `activeFloor===2` (roof) the plan still shows the roof diaphragm (374, parapets included) unchanged, and 1-story mode is untouched (`displayPlf` null). Engine guard not run this session at the user's request (display-only change, no guarded fn touched); esbuild compile clean. `APP_BUILD = 114` ("Version 1.14"). See ┬¦4ii.

> **rev 29 ŌĆö DEPLOYED TO VERCEL (Vite host scaffold; NO app-code change).** The app is now a deployed static site (GitHub web UI ŌåÆ Vercel auto-deploy). > **rev 27 ŌĆö TWO-STORY: STEP 6 ARM-AWARE VERTICAL LOAD STACKING (landed).** The 1st-floor shear walls now carry the upper story's overturning with the correct moment arm. Because Step 5 already handed each floor the right force AND design height, the arm-aware base moment is exactly the SUM of the two floors' engine overturning moments for the same vertically-aligned segment: **M_base = Mot(1st) + Mot(2nd)** (e.g. roof 5k @ 20ft + 2nd-floor 6k @ 10ft over a 10ft wall ŌåÆ (5┬Ę20+6┬Ę10)/10 = **16k**, NOT a flat 11k). **Standing rules for every session (do these automatically, without being asked):**
- **Preview on resume.** As soon as you've read this handoff, preview the current `plan-sketcher-suite.jsx` in chat ŌĆö copy it to `/mnt/user-data/outputs/` and present it so it renders as a live artifact ŌĆö *before* writing the state summary and waiting for a task. The user wants to see the live app at the start of every session.
- **Run the test harness ONCE per chat, at the start.** After the preview, set up the harness (┬¦6b) and run it a single time at the **beginning of the session** on the current code to establish a clean baseline (build + comment-lexer + render smoke + the engine byte-identity guard + whatever targeted suites exist). **Do NOT re-run the full sweep after every individual edit** ŌĆö that burns tokens. Per change, the minimal guard is: esbuild compile, the engine byte-identity check (cheap, pure-Python), and a focused render/headless smoke for the *specific* thing you touched. Snapshot the engine baseline (`cp work/plan-sketcher-suite.jsx work/.engine-baseline.jsx`) as part of that one session-start run, before your first edit.
- **Handoff tracks code.** Any time the app is updated, update this MD in the **same session/response** as the code. That means: bump the rev line at the very top, add a new `┬¦4*`-style rev subsection describing the change (additive/invariant tone, like the existing ones), update the rev number inside the ┬¦0 resume prompt, and adjust "Where rev N left off" / "Open items". Never hand back updated code with a stale handoff ŌĆö the two always ship together.
- **Version bump.** On every app update, increment `APP_BUILD` by 1 at the top of the jsx (rev 25 introduced it at 100 = "Version 1.00", shown in the top bar). It rolls 199ŌåÆ"2.00" by construction. This is the user-facing version ONLY ŌĆö never touch `CURRENT_VERSION` (save-file schema) to bump the display.

**Save-file status (as of rev 29):** the app is now **deployed to Vercel (rev 29)**, but the Save/Open (`.wps`) feature **has not been used in anger yet** ŌĆö so **no real save files exist in the wild that could break.** The rev 23ŌĆō24 forward-compat work and the save-file regression guards are therefore *pre-emptive insurance*, not protecting live data. Practical consequence: when adding fields, you still want the merge-on-defaults discipline so a future save round-trips, but you do **not** need to treat "an old `.wps` won't load" as a live-fire risk yet. (This stops being true the moment someone saves a real `.wps` from the live site ŌĆö once the two-story sign-off below happens, assume real files may start to exist.)

## 1. What this app is

A merged React app (one JSX file, rendered as a Claude artifact, deployed via GitHub web UI ŌåÆ Vercel) with **three tabs** (leftŌåÆright, sheet numbers S-1/S-2/S-3): **Plan Sketcher ┬Ę Design ┬Ę Calculation Sheet**.

1. **Plan Sketcher** ŌĆö dark-theme SVG plan editor. Draw a building footprint (straight walls only, 1 unit = 1 ft), drag wind sections across it, and it computes ASCE-style wind **line loads (plf)** on windward walls and **point-load reactions (kips)** on walls parallel to the wind, via simply-supported beam statics.
2. **Design** ŌĆö plan-view shear-wall designer fed by the sketcher. Each point-load wall arrives as a "line" (length, wall height H, reaction lbs). Per-line optimizer (`generateDesign`), drag-in-plan shear walls with live recalc, right-click overrides (holdown / edge nailing type / end post) validated against engine capacities.
3. **Calculation Sheet** ŌĆö verbatim port of "Plywood Shear Wall ŌĆö Wood Studs.xlsx" (engine `calcSegment` is character-identical to the source app). **Now styled LIGHT, 1:1 with the standalone calculator**: paper page + white sheet w/ ink border, light title block w/ ŌÄÖ Print button, compliance banner (clickable per-wall verdicts), D/C utilization bars, collapsible sections w/ fail badges, sticky row labels, zebra/hover, column highlight (click SW-n header / elevation wall / banner chip), formula-cell tooltips on row labels. **Do not change its logic or row labels without asking the user.**

The user (licensed PE/SE) replaces commercial spreadsheets (Struware) with these tools. **Rule from the user: never delete existing functionality ŌĆö ask first. Additions only unless instructed.**

| ~100ŌĆō330 | **load engine**: `findLeewardPartner`, `lineReactions` (beam statics), `buildSecData` (windward grouping, leeward-region subdivision, dashed divides, reactions agg ŌĆö **reactions carry `key`**, `baseShear`) |
| ~480ŌĆō630 | sketcher visuals: colors `C_BG/C_WALL/C_NODE/C_LOAD/C_REACT/...`, `Tag`, `WindLoad` (renders per-region `subLoads`), `Reaction`, `SecDiagram`, `WindWindow` |
| ~640ŌĆō1140 | `PlanSketcher({ onDesignShearWalls, fileOps, registerProject })`: state, history/**future** (redo), draw mode, LENGTHEN dim editing, view fit/freeze/**auto-expand**, pointer handlers, `runDesignHandoff` |

Suite tab bar has `className="no-print"`. |

## 3. Core data model (critical to not regress)

- **Wall props** `wallProps[edgeKey] = { H, pw, qWind, qLee, par }` ŌĆö **one parapet `par` per physical wall** (legacy `parW` auto-migrated in `propsFor`). The leeward parapet term is **read live from the actual back wall** via `findLeewardPartner(windKey, axis, sign, graph, sAt)`; `sAt` = across-wind cut position so split back walls resolve to the segment behind *this* cut. **(rev 14) The leeward *wall height* is handled the same way**: it is the back wall's own `H`, surfaced in the section-cut window as `activeSection.leeH` and edited via `setVals("lee",{H})`. No new stored field ŌĆö each physical wall keeps one `H`, so reversing the wind/cutting from the other side just swaps roles and the heights stick. The leeward wall height feeds the **elevation diagram only** (sloping roof); it does **not** enter this wall's plf (the windward `H` drives the line load ŌĆö the back wall's `H` drives *its* line load when it is the windward face).
- **plf formula** per windward region: `0.5┬ĘH┬Ępw + par┬ĘqWind + leePar(region)┬ĘqLee`. A windward wall is **subdivided where the back wall changes** (`buildSecData` ŌåÆ `w.subLoads`, dashed `divides`, true `baseShear`). The dashed `divides` are drawn only where plf actually changes; **rev 18** makes the on-plan plf *label* match ŌĆö `WindLoad` coalesces consecutive equal-plf sub-spans into ONE label, so two values appear only when the load genuinely differs (e.g. a 374|462 south wall), never as a duplicated 374|374.
- **Reactions**: collinear windward segments group into a *line*; the line is a beam on the point-load (support) walls; per-bay simply-supported statics (`W┬Ę(TLŌłÆX)/TL`), loads split at interior supports, **overhangs ŌåÆ nearest support**. Splitting a wall with equal props never changes reactions (invariant, tested). A wall qualifies as a support if it runs parallel to the wind, sits within the line's across-wind span, and is **at or downwind of the windward face** (`lineReactions`, rev 18) ŌĆö it need NOT span all the way back to the windward depth, so a **re-entrant interior wall** (the step wall of an L, a notch wall) acts as an interior support exactly like a full-depth interior wall. Only walls entirely *upwind* of the windward face are rejected (they belong to a deeper windward line in a concave footprint).
- **Elevation window**: opens on the exact windward segment the cut crosses (lowest-`t` hit); a valid cut must cross **Ōēź2 across-wind walls**. Reverse flips sign and re-opens the segment at the same across-wind position. `setVals("self"|"lee", patch)` writes to the wall the value physically belongs to.
- **Design handoff** (`runDesignHandoff`, shared by card + ribbon buttons): per reaction (kips>0) ŌåÆ line `{id:"ax|key", key, windAxis, o, a, b, lengthFt (full collinear extent), heightFt (max H along it), forceLbs (kips├Ś1000)}` + a frozen copy of the footprint. Parapets are **not** sent.
- **Design engine per line**: `lineResults(line, segs, g, d)` runs `calcSegment` with `gLine={...g, wWind:line.forceLbs}`, `totalL = ╬Ż seg lengths on the line`. Overrides per seg `s.ov = {type?, hd?, post?}`; NG flags via `hdCapacity` (uplift Ōēź cap) and `postAllowable` (comp > Pa, thin-wall 4x6 = `Pa46┬Ę3.5/5.5`). Constraints `d` are **global across lines** (deliberate; per-line constraints = possible future ask).

## 4. UI features added this session (all additive)

- **Ribbon toolbar** (in PlanSketcher, above canvas): File (New/Open/Save), Edit (Undo/**Redo**/Clear), Draft (Ō£Å Draw / ŌīŚ Snap / Ōł¤ Ortho / Ō¤Ę Dims toggles), View (ŌŖĪ Fit / + In / ŌłÆ Out), **Markup (on-plan markup-scale dropdown 1├Ś / 0.75├Ś / 0.5├Ś / 0.25├Ś ŌĆö scales text + arrows + nodes together; rev 32 ┬¦4gg, was "Text" rev 30)**, Stories (1-Story/2-Story pill), Analyze (ŌÜĪ Design shear walls ŌĆö disabled until reactions exist). Presets live in the side panel (deduped out of the ribbon, rev 5). Side-panel cards otherwise intentionally duplicated, not removed.
- **Status bar** (below canvas): live cursor X/Y in ft (gated setState), mode badge `SELECT` / `DRAW ┬Ę chaining`, clickable SNAP/ORTHO flags, right side = walls ┬Ę total ft ┬Ę EŌĆōW/NŌĆōS base shears.
- **Draw mode**: polyline clicking; node snap (radius `2.4┬ĘS`, cyan ring, **beats ortho** ŌĆö CAD osnap) closes loops exactly; ortho locks H/V from anchor; grid snap; yellow dashed rubber band with live length; right-click ends chain, Esc ends chain then exits mode; duplicate edges rejected; each placement undoable. While ON, all clicks place points (drag/cut/dim-edit suspended).
- **LENGTHEN dim editing**: end nearest the click moves (`t` projection, ┬▒10% midband ŌåÆ anchor the **higher-degree** node); `applyWallLength(edge, len, moveEnd)`; ortho propagation follows the moved end.
- **View**: auto-fit; frozen during drags; **auto-expands** (`expandViewTo`, pointer+5% margin) so one gesture reaches any distance; pointer capture keeps drags alive outside the SVG.
- **Shortcuts**: Ctrl+S/O save/open, Ctrl+Z undo, Ctrl+Shift+Z or Ctrl+Y redo, Esc/Delete as before.
- **.wps project file** (version 1): `{app:"plan-sketcher-suite", version:1, savedAt, sketcher:{graph, wallProps, noSupport[], sections, nextId}, design:{lines, shape, segsByLine, d}, calc:{g, segments}}`. Sketcher registers `get/set` via `registerProject`; shell owns Blob download / FileReader open / New (confirm). Open restores everything and clears undo/redo.

## 4k. Rev 11 ŌĆö Design-constraints panel rebuilt for alignment + height (user screenshot of the panel, asked: align inputs, smaller text, shorter pinned panel)

Root-cause from the close-up: (a) controls didn't align ŌĆö number inputs fixed 56px, selects wider/variable, ragged within and across cards; (b) the panel was TALL because every field stacked label-ABOVE-control (2 lines) ├Ś 3 rows. Font size was a red herring ŌĆö the stacking was the cost.

**New field system** (replaces ConGroup/SwField/conSel/conNum usage in the panel; those helpers are now unused but left defined):
- `PinCard({title, cols})` ŌĆö card with a real CSS grid (`repeat(cols, minmax(0,1fr))`, columnGap 12, rowGap 5). Loads + Dimensions are `cols=2`; Plywood + Other are `cols=1`.
- `PinRow({label, unit, full, grow})` ŌĆö INLINE field: label left (8.5px uppercase, `nowrap + overflow:hidden + ellipsis + title=` so no label can ever break the row), control, then a fixed 13px unit gutter. One line per field = ~half the height of stacked. `grow` makes the control flex to fill (Plywood/Other full-width selects); default keeps control fixed so edges align in a column.
- `pinNumS` (46px, right-aligned, 11px) / `pinSelS` (minWidth 46, 11px), `PIN_H=22`.
- **Alignment** is now structural: grid columns + fixed control widths ŌåÆ every control shares a column edge.
- **Height**: stacked 3-row card (~150px) ŌåÆ inline 3-row card (~95px); panel overall ~40% shorter. Controls 24ŌåÆ22px, paddings/gaps tightened, card titles 10ŌåÆ9px.
- **Units moved labelŌåÆgutter**: "Roof DL (psf)" ŌåÆ label "Roof DL" + gutter "psf". Labels also shortened ("Max # segments"ŌåÆ"Max segs"). VALUES/bindings unchanged (`g.roofDL`, `d.*`, `setGl`/`setDk` identical).
- **Uneven flex weights** so the field-heavy cards get width and inline labels don't truncate: Loads/Dimensions `flex:1.4 1 280px` (minWidth 240), Plywood `flex:1 1 210px`, Other `flex:1 1 230px`. The ellipsis is a safety net, not the plan.
- Plywood capacity readout kept but condensed to 2 lines ("Allow. W/S (plf)", values joined by "/"). Objective stays short-labeled (rev-10) in a full-width select ŌåÆ no clip.

**Test bookkeeping** (panel DOM changed, so panel-specific assertions in older suites were retired/migrated ŌĆö NOT silently broken):
- `test_rev11_panel.cjs` (35 asserts) is the new owner of all panel structure/fields/bindings.
- `test_rev8_compact.cjs` ŌåÆ stub (its conSel/conNum/24px markers are gone; superseded by rev-11).
- `test_rev10_polish.cjs` ŌåÆ trimmed to its still-valid non-panel checks (gauges + signature).
- `test_rev7.cjs` ŌåÆ field-label arrays updated to current names ("Roof DL" not "Roof DL (psf)"); its group-card/sticky/DL-binding asserts unchanged and still pass.
- Engine: all 7 fns UNCHANGED (function-diffed vs rev 10). Sweep green: render, ribbon(rev5), rev7(24), rev8(stub), rev9(20), rev10(trimmed), rev11(35), rev6 golden+optimizer.

## 4l. Rev 12 ŌĆö Reaction "rocket" reads correctly on vertical walls (user screenshot of plan corner)

Diagnosed from a zoomed plan corner: the horizontal-wall reaction (7.29k) reads as a clean rocket because its label and arrowhead are colinear (both horizontal). The vertical-wall reaction (11.22k) pointed correctly DOWN along its wall, but its label stayed HORIZONTAL ŌåÆ a horizontal chip with an arrow poking out the bottom, not a rocket.

- **Reality check first**: ran the real `buildSecData` on the default rectangle for both wind dirs. Confirmed reactions are point loads delivered ALONG the supporting wall: secH (E-W) ŌåÆ reactions on horizontal walls pointing right (tdir {x:┬▒1,y:0}); secV (N-S) ŌåÆ reactions on vertical walls pointing down (tdir {x:0,y:┬▒1}). So the arrow DIRECTION was already correct ŌĆö only the label orientation was off.
- **Fix**: `Reaction` now computes `vert = |dy|>|dx|` and passes `rot={vert ? -90 : 0}` to `<Tag>` (Tag already supported `rot`). Vertical rockets get their label rotated -90┬░ to lie along the shaft (consistent with the -90┬░ used by WindLoad plf labels and dimension tags on vertical walls). Horizontal rockets unchanged.
- **No math touched**: `buildSecData`/`lineReactions`/`tdir`/reaction positions all identical (function-diffed). Pure presentational rotation of the label `<g>`.
- Test: `test_rev12_rocket.cjs` (6 asserts) renders `Reaction` directly for horizontal / vertical-down / vertical-up tdir and checks the label rotation (none / -90 / -90) while arrowhead + value text survive. Full sweep green; all 7 engine fns UNCHANGED.

## 4m. Rev 13 ŌĆö Shear-wall plan symbol redrawn as a drafting detail-bubble (user reference sketch)

User supplied a hand-style reference of the desired plan symbol and four asks. All presentational; lives entirely in `DesignPlan` (the per-segment `<g>` in the `lines.map`) plus three small `DesignTab` wiring lines.

- **Detail-bubble callout (type + length).** The old single text label `SW-n ┬Ę LŌĆ▓ ┬Ę Type n Ō£Ģ` above the band is gone. In its place: an inverted (point-down) triangle floats above the wall center on a short stem, holding **just the type number** (e.g. `1`, not `Type 1`) via `isNum(r.selType) ? r.selType : "ŌĆö"`. The **length** (`fmt(s.length,2)ŌĆ▓`) is dimensioned on its own line **above** the triangle. Triangle constants: `tipOff=band+1.3*S`, `triH=2.3*S`, `triHalf=1.35*S`; type at `triH*0.56` up from apex, length `1.05*S` above the base. All three (stem/triangle geometry via `at()`) auto-orient to the wall; the two text nodes get the usual `vert?rotate(-90)` readability spin.
- **Half-width band.** `band` 2.4*S ŌåÆ **1.2*S** (the only line-level constant change), giving the thin-band look of the reference. Hatch `step` 1.8*S ŌåÆ 1.3*S and lighter weight so density reads right on the thinner band. Note `band` is tied to building size (S = maxVB/110), NOT wall length ŌĆö same scaling idiom as before, just halved.
- **End zones = X-boxes (not solid posts).** Each end is now an **outlined** square (`fill C_BG`, half-size `eb=band`) with two diagonals forming an X ŌĆö the boundary/post symbol from the reference ŌĆö replacing the old solid `fill={stroke}` square. The separate visible stretch-handle rect was dropped; the transparent hit-circle (`r=1.5*S`, `onPointerDown` L/R) is retained so **drag-to-stretch still works**, and the body polygon still drag-slides (M), and the `<g onContextMenu>` right-click override is unchanged.
- **Dot bubble now numbered = the hold-down number.** The end holdown indicator is kept and still gated on `r.dispHd && !=="None"`, but is now a **filled** circle (`fill={stroke}`, white ring) centered on the end box carrying the **HDU model number** parsed from `dispHd` via `/HDU(\d+)/` (HDU4ŌåÆ`4`, HDU11ŌåÆ`11`; wood `(2) HDU4`ŌåÆ`4`; `NG!`ŌåÆ`!`). Font shrinks for 2-digit. Color scheme deliberately **kept** (blue pass / red fail) ŌĆö did NOT adopt the reference's yellow.
- **SW tag now toggled, off by default.** The `SW-A/B/ŌĆ”` mark no longer renders automatically. `DesignTab` gained `const [showTags,setShowTags]=useState(false)` and a **"Show/Hide wall tags"** button in the plan's `SectionTitle` right-slot (`swBtn(showTags)`); `showTags` flows to `DesignPlan` as a prop and gates a tag text node placed **below** the wall (`at(mid, band+1.5*S)`), so it never collides with the length above.
- **No math touched**: engine guard re-run by building engine-export bundles from baseline AND current and deep-comparing `schedFor` (both grades), `calcSegment`, and `generateDesign` on fixed inputs ŌåÆ all IDENTICAL. Compile + SSR render smoke (6/6) green. Verified the symbol visually by rasterizing the exact geometry standalone (resvg) at realistic S ŌĆö passing/failing/no-holdown walls + tags all read correctly, incl. vertical rotation.

## 4n. Rev 14 ŌĆö Leeward wall height + sloping roof line (user-requested)

User ask: "add a height value to the leeward wall in the section cut windowŌĆ” the roof line can be slopingŌĆ” change the leeward height no matter the direction of the section cut." Implemented as a presentational/UI + live-read change; **no engine touch, no new stored field, `.wps` schema untouched**.

- **Leeward height = back wall's own `H`** (mirrors the leeward-parapet pattern exactly). `activeSection` now also returns `leeH: lee ? lee.H : 0` (read via the existing `activeLeeKey`/`findLeewardPartner`). `WindWindow` seeds a `leeH` field and routes its edits with a new `upd` branch `prop==="leeH" ŌåÆ setVals("lee",{ H:num(raw) })` (writes to the back wall, alongside the existing `parL ŌåÆ setVals("lee",{par})`). Because each physical wall keeps one `H`, this works through reverse and through split back walls, and is settable from either cut direction ŌĆö satisfying "no matter the direction."
- **`SecDiagram` redrawn for a sloping roof.** Old single flat `H`/`roofY` replaced by independent `HL=v.H` (windward) and `HR=v.leeH` (leeward) with a **common foundation baseline** `wallBot=padTop+availH`; `roofYL/roofYR` are each side's roof point. The wall is now a `<polygon>` trapezoid (left edge HL, right edge HR, sloped top); the ROOF LINE label rotates to the slope angle (`roofAng=atan2(roofYR-roofYL, wallRX-wallLX)`). Each parapet column + its pressure arrows hang off its own side's roof point (`parWTop=roofYL-ŌĆ”`, `parLTop=roofYR-ŌĆ”`). Scaling `maxFt=max(HL+parW, HR+parL, 1)`. **Backward-compatible: when `HL===HR` the geometry is pixel-identical to the old flat diagram** (verified ŌĆö `roofYL===roofYR`, angle 0).
- **New editable box**: a red leeward-wall height box (`field="leeH" prop="leeH"`) at the leeward wall mid-height, beside the existing windward `H` box. Windward `H` box nudged to `wallLX+22` for symmetry with `wallRX-22`.
- **Total line-load breakdown unchanged** (Wall H/2┬Ępw + windward parapet + leeward parapet) ŌĆö leeward *wall* height is geometric context, not a term in this wall's plf.
- **Verification**: esbuild syntax OK, comment-lexer clean, render smoke 7/7. **Engine guard** (fresh export bundles from the pre-edit baseline vs current, deep-compare `schedFor`/`calcSegment`/`generateDesign` both grades) ŌåÆ ALL IDENTICAL. New `test_slope` (7 asserts): sloped both directions (windward-taller and leeward-taller), ROOF LINE rotated, both height boxes render their values, and the flat `HL===HR` case has zero slope. SVG emitted + confirmed well-formed (cairosvg rasterizes blank here ŌĆö its marker/defs handling, not a code issue; geometry asserted via SSR instead).

## 4p. Rev 16 ŌĆö Design height label HŌåÆh + section-cut parapet redrawn as line-with-node (user-requested)

Two independent UI-only asks, both presentational; engine + all logic byte-identical (guard CLEAN vs baseline).

- **Design-tab height label `H ŌåÆ h`.** The rev-15 row is now `<Row label="Wall height h" unit="ft" ŌĆ”>` (was `"Wall height H"`). Reason from the user: lowercase `h` is the height symbol in the aspect-ratio formula `h/L`, and that row (`"Aspect ratio h/L"`) sits immediately below ŌĆö so the two now read consistently. Pure string change; value/binding (`sel.heightFt`) untouched. (First-letter-capitalization rule from ┬¦4d is unaffected ŌĆö the changed `h` is mid-string.)
- **Section-cut parapets are now a LINE, not a column rectangle** (`SecDiagram`, Plan Sketcher tab). Each parapet was a `<rect width={colW=26}>` column standing on its side's roof point; it is now a single vertical `<line>` continuing the wall's outer face upward ŌĆö windward at `x=wallLX` from `roofYLŌåÆparWTop`, leeward at `x=wallRX` from `roofYRŌåÆparLTop`. The `colW` const was removed (its only consumers were the two rects, the two labels, and the two height boxes ŌĆö all re-anchored).
- **WINDWARD / LEEWARD labels** keep their vertical (`rotate(-90)`) orientation but now sit *beside* the parapet line (interior side: `wallLX+8` / `wallRX-8`) instead of centered inside the old column. Still gated on `parW>0` / `parL>0`.
- **Node where the parapet starts.** A small filled `<circle r=2.4 fill={C_NODE} stroke="#FFFFFF">` is drawn at the wall/parapet junction ŌĆö windward `(wallLX, roofYL)`, leeward `(wallRX, roofYR)`. Because that point is `wallBot ŌłÆ H┬ĘpxPerFt` (and `pxPerFt` rescales off `maxFt`), the node **repositions live** as any height (wall or parapet, either side) is typed ŌĆö no new state, it's derived from the existing live values. Gated on the parapet existing.
- **Parapet height boxes** (red, `fmt1(par) ft`) re-anchored off the removed `colW` to the line: windward `wallLX+30`, leeward `wallRX-30` (clears the beside-line label). Pressure-arrow geometry, the wall trapezoid, the sloping ROOF LINE label, and both wall-height boxes are all unchanged ŌĆö the flat-roof (`HL===HR`) case still degrades to the prior pixel geometry apart from rectŌåÆline.
- **Verification**: esbuild syntax OK, comment-lexer clean, render smoke 6/6, engine guard CLEAN (7 fns byte-identical vs baseline). New `test_secdiagram_parapet.cjs` (13 asserts) renders `SecDiagram` directly across three cases ŌĆö both parapets present (asserts WINDWARD/LEEWARD text, both `<circle>` nodes at cx 95/250 with white ring, both parapet `<line>`s with `x1==x2`, **no** `width="26"` column rect, polygon + ROOF LINE intact, `5 ft`/`4 ft` value boxes), flat-roof (nodes present, no column), and no-parapet (no line/node/label). Note `fmt1` rounds to integer when whole (`5`, not `5.0`) ŌĆö assert on `5 ft`.

## 4r. Rev 18 ŌĆö Re-entrant interior walls take point loads + equal-plf labels merge (user screenshots: L-shape vs rectangle)

User showed an L-shape (20ft step wall `2-3`, 23ft wall `1-2`) beside a rectangle with an interior wall, and asked: (a) the re-entrant walls should take **point-load reactions** like the rectangle's interior wall does, and (b) the left wall shows **"374 plf" twice** with no real load change ŌĆö two values should appear only where the load actually differs along the wall (like the 374|462 south wall).

- **Root cause (a):** `lineReactions` gate 4 required a support wall to *reach the windward line's depth* (`line.depth Ōłł [aMin,aMax]`). The L's 20ft step wall sits at x60ŌĆō80 while the windward (left) wall is at x20, so it failed the test and carried nothing in EŌĆōW wind. (In NŌĆōS wind the 23ft wall already worked ŌĆö it spans its windward line's depth.) **Fix:** the gate is now `aMax < line.depth ŌłÆ tol ŌåÆ skip`, i.e. a support need only be **at or downwind of the windward face**; a re-entrant wall tied to that face by the diaphragm is an interior support. One line changed in `lineReactions`; the parallel-to-wind and across-wind-span gates are unchanged.
- **Root cause (b):** `buildSecData` subdivides a windward wall at every back-wall breakpoint into `w.subLoads`; `WindLoad` rendered one label per sub-load, so an equal-plf split showed a duplicate label even though the dashed `divides` (which test `|╬öplf|>0.5`) correctly drew nothing. **Fix:** `WindLoad` now coalesces consecutive equal-plf sub-spans (`|╬öplf|<0.5`) into one span before rendering ŌĆö **display-only**, no engine/statics/`divides` touched (`subLoads` is read nowhere else; grep-confirmed).
- **Effect on the L-shape (EŌĆōW wind):** step wall `2-3` now carries the dominant point load. Before 8.41/8.41k (top/bottom only); after **top 4.30k ┬Ę step 8.41k ┬Ę bottom 4.11k** (╬ŻŌēł16.83k = the line load ŌĆö balances). NŌĆōS wind unchanged (left 7.48 ┬Ę 23ft wall `1-2` 11.22 ┬Ę `3-4` 3.74k). Rectangle + interior wall unchanged (4.67 / 11.22 / 6.54k).
- **Side effect, flagged to user:** a **U-shape** in EŌĆōW wind now also loads the notch-bottom wall as an interior support (8.41/8.41 ŌåÆ **5.61/8.41/2.81k**, still balances). Arguably more correct (base diaphragm ties it to the windward face); reversible if undesired.
- **Verification:** syntax OK ┬Ę comment-lexer clean ┬Ę render smoke 5/5 ┬Ę **engine guard CLEAN** ŌĆö `calcSegment/generateDesign/evaluateCandidate/baseDesignSeg/lineResults/buildSecData/computeCut/findLeewardPartner/pointInRing` all byte-identical (only `lineReactions` + `WindLoad` changed, both intended). New regression `work/test_reentrant_reactions.cjs` (9/9: step wall is the dominant reaction & totals balance; NŌĆōS + rectangle unchanged; left-wall sub-loads equal ŌåÆ merge). `WindLoad` SSR (4/4): equal plf ŌåÆ one label, 374|462 ŌåÆ two labels.

## 4s. Rev 19 ŌĆö CAD navigation + Draw stops auto-zooming the canvas (user report: first node jumps to center, canvas keeps zooming while drawing; asked for mouse-wheel zoom like CAD)

The viewBox was `frozenView || fit`, where `fit` is a `useMemo` that auto-frames the bounding box of all nodes on every `graph` change. In Draw mode nothing froze the view, so each click re-fit the canvas ŌĆö and the **first** node collapsed `fit` to a ~20├Ś20 ft window centred on that node (the "spawns at center + keeps zooming" report).

- **New view model:** added a persistent **`userView`** state; `view = frozenView || userView || fit` (auto-fit only when `userView` is null). `viewRef`/`userViewRef` keep the live values for handlers. `freezeView` now freezes the *current* view (incl. manual zoom), and `expandViewTo` grows from it ŌĆö so drags start from wherever you're zoomed, not from `fit`.
- **Draw no longer refits:** entering Draw seeds `userView` from the current view (`toggleDrawMode`). Placing a node only ever **grows** the view to keep the new node visible (`growUserViewTo` ŌĆö expand-only, never recenters/zooms-in); a node inside the view leaves it untouched. So the canvas holds still while you chain walls, and still lets you draw past the old viewport edge.
- **CAD navigation:** mouse **wheel = zoom toward the cursor** (`zoomAt`, native non-passive `wheel` listener so page-scroll is prevented; keeps the world point under the cursor fixed, preserves aspect, clamps span to `VMIN 6 ŌĆ” VMAX 3┬ĘWORLD` ft). **Middle-drag = pan** (`panRef`; the native middle-button autoscroll puck is suppressed). New **View** ribbon group: **ŌŖĪ Fit** (`zoomToFit` ŌåÆ `userView=null`, zoom-extents) + **+ In / ŌłÆ Out** buttons (zoom about the canvas centre) for trackpad/no-wheel users. Loading a preset / New / opening a file resets `userView=null` so the plan re-frames.
- **No engine/geometry/statics touched.** Function-diff vs the rev-18 file: `calcSegment / generateDesign / evaluateCandidate / baseDesignSeg / lineResults / buildSecData / lineReactions / WindLoad / Reaction / computeCut / findLeewardPartner / pointInRing` all byte-identical ŌĆö the change is entirely the view state + pointer/wheel handlers + three ribbon buttons + a help line.
- **Verification:** syntax OK ┬Ę comment-lexer clean ┬Ę render smoke 5/5 (App still mounts; View buttons present in the rendered ribbon) ┬Ę navigation **math invariants** (`/tmp/view_math.cjs`, 14/14): zoom keeps the cursor world-point fixed & preserves aspect, zoom-in/out clamp at VMIN/VMAX, **grow leaves the view unchanged when the point is already inside (the no-jump guarantee)** and expands-only otherwise, pan translates without resizing ┬Ę rev-18 reaction regression still 9/9.

## 4t. Rev 20 ŌĆö Pan tool + wheel-zoom toggle on the empty-area right-click menu (user-requested)

User asked to add a left-drag **Pan** capability and surface it (plus Draw and a wheel-zoom switch) on the right-click of empty canvas, **without disturbing the existing right-click menus** (node = select/connect/delete; wall = point-load/add-node/delete) or the draw-chain right-click.

- **New "Canvas" context menu.** `onBgContextMenu` previously just cleared the selection on empty-area right-click. It still does that (and still ends the draw chain when in Draw mode ŌĆö that path is untouched), but when **not** drawing it now also calls `openMenu(e,{kind:"canvas"})`. The menu render gained a third branch (`menu.kind==="canvas"`) ahead of the existing node/wall branches: **Ō£Å Draw** (calls `toggleDrawMode`), **Ō£ŗ Pan** (`togglePanMode`), and **­¤öŹ Zoom (wheel)** with a status dot. Draw/Pan show a Ō£ō + active tint when on; the menu closes on Draw/Pan but **stays open on Zoom** so the light visibly flips.
- **Pan tool (`panMode`).** A left-drag "hand" tool that complements the existing middle-drag pan (rev 19) for trackpad/no-middle-button users. New `beginPan(e)` starts the **same** `panRef` gesture the middle button uses (capture ŌåÆ translate `userView` in `onMove` ŌåÆ release in `onUp`), so panning math is shared and unchanged. All three left-button entry points route to it when `panMode` is on: `onBgLDown`, `onNodeLDown`, `onWallLDown` (and dimension labels), so dragging **anywhere** pans instead of moving geometry / cutting a section / opening the dim editor. Mutually exclusive with Draw (each toggle clears the other). `Esc` exits Pan.
- **Wheel-zoom toggle (`zoomEnabled`, default on).** The native non-passive `wheel` listener now early-returns when `zoomEnabledRef.current` is false (so it neither zooms nor `preventDefault`s ŌĆö the page scrolls normally). The green `.cmlight` (`#34C759`, grey when off) tracks the state live. Middle-drag pan and the ŌŖĪ Fit / + In / ŌłÆ Out buttons are unaffected by this toggle.
- **Cursor + status feedback.** Canvas cursor reads `grab` in Pan mode and `grabbing` during any live pan (`panCursor` state, set on every pan start / cleared on up ŌĆö covers both middle-drag and the Pan tool). The status-bar mode chip shows **PAN** alongside the existing DRAW / SELECT.
- **No engine/geometry/statics touched.** Tail-diff vs the rev-19 file from `function calcSegment` to EOF is **byte-identical**; `lineReactions / buildSecData / findLeewardPartner` unchanged in place. All edits are confined to the `PlanSketcher` view/interaction layer (state + refs, pointer/wheel handlers, the canvas menu branch, three CSS rules, the help line) above the shear module.
- **Verification:** TypeScript TSX parse clean (no syntax diagnostics) ┬Ę single-declaration check for every new identifier (`panMode/zoomEnabled/panCursor/panModeRef/zoomEnabledRef/beginPan/togglePanMode`) ┬Ę engine tail byte-identical guard passed.

## 4u. Rev 21 ŌĆö Canvas menu reachable mid-draw (user-requested)

Rev 20 left the empty-area Canvas menu unreachable while in Draw mode, because `onBgContextMenu` short-circuited to `endDrawChain()` on every right-click in Draw. User asked to make the menu reachable mid-draw **without** losing the right-click-ends-the-chain behavior.

- **Two-stage right-click in Draw mode.** `onBgContextMenu` now branches on `drawAnchorRef.current`: if a chain is **active** (anchor ŌēĀ null) the first right-click ends it exactly as before (muscle memory preserved); if **no chain is active** (anchor null ŌĆö you just ended one, or haven't started) the right-click opens `openMenu(e,{kind:"canvas"})`. So a quick double-right-click = end chain ŌåÆ menu, and right-clicking before drawing anything opens the menu immediately. The non-Draw path (clear selection ŌåÆ open menu) is unchanged.
- **In-Draw the menu is self-consistent.** The Canvas branch already renders **Ō£Å Draw** with the active Ō£ō tint, so opening it mid-draw shows Draw lit and one click toggles Draw off; picking **Ō£ŗ Pan** swaps DrawŌåÆPan (mutually exclusive); the **Zoom** light still flips in place. Nothing new in the menu render ŌĆö only the gate that reaches it.
- **No engine/geometry/statics touched.** Tail-diff from `function calcSegment` to EOF is **byte-identical** vs rev 20. The whole change is the `onBgContextMenu` branch + one help-line word; 11 changed lines total, all in the `PlanSketcher` view layer.
- **Verification:** TypeScript TSX parse clean ┬Ę engine-tail byte-identical guard passed ┬Ę change scope = 11 lines.

## 4v. Rev 22 ŌĆö Full session restore: a reopened `.wps` looks like where you left off (user-requested)

User: *"if I load a save file, it looks like when I just left the last time I was working on it."* Rev 21 and earlier saved **inputs + geometry only** and threw away the working view on load ŌĆö `onFileChosen` forced `setTab("plan")`, and the sketcher's `set()` nulled `userView` (re-fit) and cleared selection/mode. So reopening dropped you on the Plan tab, auto-framed, nothing selected, regardless of where you were. This rev makes the file a **full session snapshot** while staying byte-compatible with old files.

- **Schema bumped to `version:2`** (additive). New pieces: a top-level `ui:{ tab, hlSel }` slice; `design.selLine`; and the sketcher slice now also carries the camera + working state. Full v2 shape: `sketcher:{ graph, wallProps, noSupport[], sections, nextId, view, selected, drawMode, panMode, zoomEnabled, snapOn, ortho, dims }`, `design:{ lines, shape, segsByLine, d, selLine }`, `calc:{ g, segments }`, `ui:{ tab, hlSel }`.
- **`registerProject.get()`** now also emits `view:viewRef.current` (the live viewBox = exact zoom/pan), `selected:selRef.current` (highlighted node), `drawMode/panMode/zoomEnabled` (nav mode) and the `snapOn/ortho/dims` toolbar toggles.
- **`registerProject.set()`** restores them **feature-detected**: `setUserView(s.view || null)` (present ŌćÆ exact camera; absent ŌćÆ the old auto-fit), `setFrozenView(null)`, `setSelected("selected" in s ? ŌĆ” : null)`, `setDrawMode/ŌĆŗsetPanMode`, `setZoomEnabled("zoomEnabled" in s ? ŌĆ” : true)`, and `if("snapOn"/"ortho"/"dims" in s)` for the toggles. v1 files (and **New**, whose `set()` payload has no `view`) therefore behave exactly as before ŌĆö auto-fit, defaults ŌĆö so nothing regressed.
- **Tab/selection restored last, not forced.** `onFileChosen` now ends with `setHlSel(p.ui&&"hlSel"in p.ui?ŌĆ”:null)` then `setTab(p.ui&&p.ui.tab?p.ui.tab:"plan")` ŌĆö v2 lands on the saved tab, v1 still lands on Plan. Design state is set before the tab in the same handler so React batches them and the Design tab paints with its lines already present (no empty-flash).
- **`selLine` lifted from `DesignTab` to `App`.** It was local `useState` in `DesignTab`, which **unmounts** on every tab switch (only `PlanSketcher` stays mounted via `display:none`; Design/Calc are `{tab===ŌĆ” && ŌĆ”}`), so the selected line couldn't survive a save/load. Now `App` owns `selLine/setSelLine`, passes them as props, and the sketcherŌåÆdesign handoff seeds it (`setSelLine(prev => lines.find(l=>l.id===prev) ? prev : lines[0]?.id ?? null)` ŌĆö keeps a still-valid selection, else first line). `DesignTab`'s existing validity effect is unchanged.
- **Deliberately NOT restored** (transient/edit-in-progress, jarring to auto-reopen): the modal **wind line-load window** (`activeWall`) and the inline **dimension editor** (`dimEdit`) ŌĆö both stay closed, their underlying data is fully restored, one click reopens. **Undo/redo history** is still cleared on load (a loaded file is a fresh history root) ŌĆö cross-session undo is out of scope.
- **Engine untouched.** No calc/statics/optimizer code changed; the byte-identity guard over `calcSegment, generateDesign, evaluateCandidate, lineResults, withUtil, buildSecData, lineReactions` is **CLEAN**. Change is confined to App save/open + the sketcher `get/set` + the `selLine` lift.
- **Verification:** esbuild bundle clean ┬Ę engine guard CLEAN ┬Ę render smoke (plan) + SSR mount on all three tab variants pass ┬Ę new `test_savestate.cjs` contract suite **24/24** (asserts the save shape, every `get()` field, the feature-detected `set()` restores + v1 fallbacks, the open-time tab/selLine restore, and that `selLine` is lifted). *Env note: this session's box had no network, so the ┬¦6b `npm install react@18` step wasn't possible; react/react-dom **19** (already present globally) were used for the SSR smokes via `NODE_PATH` ŌĆö fine for landmark/mount checks. A normal ┬¦6b setup with react@18 is still the intended harness.*

## 4w. Rev 23 ŌĆö Save-file forward-compat hardening (user question: "is there any chance an old save file won't load correctly into an updated version of the app?")

The honest answer was *yes, for one class of change*: the loader **replaces** `g`/`d`/`segments`/per-wall props wholesale (`setG(p.calc.g)`, `setD(p.design.d)`, `setSegments(p.calc.segments)`, `setWallProps(s.wallProps||{})`), so a field ADDED to any of those in a future rev would come back `undefined` on an OLD file (a latent NaN / blank-control risk). The sketcher's *UI-state* restore was already feature-detected and safe (rev 22); this rev fixes the wholesale-replaced **data** objects. Three moves, all additive, **behavior byte-identical for every existing v1 AND v2 file** and the save shape is unchanged.

- **(1) Merge onto named defaults.** The inline `useState` literals for `g` and `d`, and the per-segment shape inside `mkSeg`, were hoisted verbatim to module-scope `DEFAULT_G` / `DEFAULT_D` / `SEG_DEFAULTS` (values + key order proven identical to the prior literals ŌĆö a "hoist fidelity" test, 6/6). The loader now merges: `setG({...DEFAULT_G, ...calc.g})`, `setD({...DEFAULT_D, ...design.d})`, `setSegments(calc.segments.map(s=>({...SEG_DEFAULTS, ...s})))`. For a *complete* current object the merge is a no-op (it overrides every default key); it only fills keys an OLD file lacks. **Per-wall props** get the same treatment via a new module-scope `mergeWallProps(p)` that subsumes the old legacy-`parW` shim and then merges onto `DEF_SECTION`; `propsFor` is now a one-liner calling it. *Sections* (`{axis,sign}`) are identity-only objects (always fully constructed) so they need no merge ŌĆö left as-is. *`g.grade` was deliberately NOT added to `DEFAULT_G`*: the engine treats a falsy grade as "rated", so omitting it keeps the save shape unchanged and current files byte-identical (a one-line change if you later want new saves to carry `grade:"rated"` explicitly).
- **(2) Real `version` gate + migration ladder.** The `version` tag was written but never read. Added `CURRENT_VERSION = 2`, a `MIGRATIONS` step table (`MIGRATIONS[k]` takes a project at version k ŌåÆ k+1; `1ŌåÆ2` is a no-op stamp since v2 is purely additive), a `migrateProject(raw)` that walks the version up one step at a time and reports `newer` when the file was saved by a future build, and a **"saved by a newer version ŌĆö some data may not load correctly"** `window.alert` on that case. `onSave` now stamps `version:CURRENT_VERSION`. The 1ŌåÆ2 step does no data transform on purpose (the additive loader already tolerates absent v2 fields) ŌĆö the ladder exists so the NEXT (possibly breaking) change has a home: `MIGRATIONS[2] = p => ({...rewrite, version:3})`.
- **(3) Pure `loadProject(raw)` + fixture-based load-regression test.** The migrateŌåÆmerge logic lives in a module-scope pure `loadProject(raw)` that returns ready-to-dispatch slices (`{newer, project, calc:{g,segments}, design:{lines,shape,segsByLine,d,selLine}, ui:{tab,hlSel}}`) **preserving the loader's exact present-checks** (g/segments/d applied only when present; tab/hlSel/selLine keep their prior fallbacks). `onFileChosen` is now a thin dispatcher over it (sketcher still restored by the sketcher's own `set()`). Because `loadProject` is pure and module-scope, the new **`test_loadstate.cjs`** loads real checked-in **`fixture_v1.wps`** + **`fixture_v2.wps`** through it and asserts the resolved state ŌĆö including the previously-untestable "real file" behavior the rev-22 contract suite couldn't reach.
- **Engine untouched.** Byte-identity guard over `calcSegment, generateDesign, evaluateCandidate, baseDesignSeg, lineResults, withUtil, buildSecData, lineReactions, findLeewardPartner, pointInRing, computeCut` is **CLEAN** (all 11 identical). `propsFor` and `mkSeg` changed by design (neither is a guarded engine fn; `buildSecData`, which *consumes* `propsFor`, is unchanged in text). Net +70 lines, all in the project-file layer + comments.
- **Verification:** esbuild bundle clean ┬Ę comment-lexer clean (no stray `*/`) ┬Ę render smoke PASS with the **plan-tab render byte-identical to baseline** (27041 chars) ┬Ę design + calc tabs SSR-mount ┬Ę engine guard CLEAN (11/11) ┬Ę **`test_loadstate.cjs` 31/31** (v2 round-trip == saved values; v1 lands on Plan w/ null ui fallbacks; a synthetic *future-field* file fills `g.wallDL`/`d.maxType`/`seg.ftgThick` from defaults instead of `undefined`; `version:99` flags `newer`; migrate ladder stamps & preserves payload; `mergeWallProps` legacy-`parW` + missing-field + no-entry cases) ┬Ę hoist-fidelity 6/6 (DEFAULT_* == prior literals, values+order; no `grade` key). *Env note: react/react-dom **18** installed via npm this session (network available) ŌĆö the intended ┬¦6b harness.*
- **To rebuild the load test in a fresh chat:** append `export { loadProject, migrateProject, DEFAULT_G, DEFAULT_D, SEG_DEFAULTS, mergeWallProps, CURRENT_VERSION };` to a *copy* of the jsx, bundle it to `work/exp.cjs` (esbuild, `--external:react --external:react-dom`), then `node work/test_loadstate.cjs` (it `require`s `work/exp.cjs` + reads the two fixtures from `work/`).

## 4x. Rev 24 ŌĆö Design-data forward-compat + a stale-line recovery path + schema guards (user: "how can we address these limits?" ŌåÆ chose **flag the Design tab stale + prompt a re-run from the saved plan** over a silent drop)

Rev 23 left two honest gaps (┬¦7): (i) `design.lines` and `segsByLine` placed segments were restored verbatim ŌĆö not merged onto defaults ŌĆö so a future per-line / per-placed-segment field would land `undefined`; (ii) the only thing that catches a *rename* or *unit* change (which merge-on-defaults can't) is discipline, which needs tooling to be reliable. This rev closes (i) and builds the tooling for (ii). **Engine byte-identical** (guard CLEAN, 11/11, vs the rev-23 baseline); all changes are in the project-file layer + a new Design-tab banner.

- **`DEFAULT_LINE` / `DEFAULT_PLACED` merge (the (i) fix).** A design LINE is `{id, key, windAxis, o, a, b, lengthFt, heightFt, forceLbs}`. Only the SCALARs are defaultable: `DEFAULT_LINE = {lengthFt:0, heightFt:13, forceLbs:0}`. The GEOMETRY (`id/key/windAxis/o/a/b`) is **deliberately NOT in a default** ŌĆö it can't be invented. Placed segments `{start, length, ov?}` merge onto `DEFAULT_PLACED = {start:0, length:0}` (`ov` rides the spread, already `(s.ov||{})`-tolerant). `loadProject` now does `lines = design.lines.map(l=>({...DEFAULT_LINE, ...l})).filter(hasGeom)` and `segsByLine[k] = arr.map(s=>({...DEFAULT_PLACED, ...s}))`, keeping **all** `segsByLine` keys (even for a filtered line, by id, so a rebuild restores its layout).
- **Stale detection + recovery (the user's choice).** `hasGeom(l)` requires a non-null `id`, two `Number.isFinite` endpoints, AND `lengthFt > 0` (lineGeom divides by `lengthFt`, so a defaulted `0` would render `NaN/Ōł×` ŌĆö this is the ┬¦6b "line lacking geometry throws on `ln.a.x`" gotcha, now caught instead of crashing). Any line failing it is **excluded**, and `loadProject` returns `design.stale = (lines.length < merged.length)`. `App` holds `designStale` (set from `L.design.stale` on open; cleared by `onDesignShearWalls` since a fresh handoff is always geometry-complete; cleared by New). `designStale` is **NOT serialized** ŌĆö a re-save after a stale load heals to the valid subset (the dropped lines were unrenderable anyway and the plan regenerates them). `DesignTab` shows an amber **"Ōå╗ Rebuild from plan"** banner (rendered at the top of BOTH return paths). The button ŌåÆ `onRebuildDesign`: if the restored plan still has a wind reaction it calls the sketcher's `rerun` (= `runDesignHandoff`, regenerates geometry-complete lines ŌåÆ `onDesignShearWalls` clears stale); otherwise it routes to the Plan with an alert to place a cut. `runDesignHandoff` + a live `hasReactions` flag are exposed to the shell on the existing `registerProject({...})` api object (the effect has no dep array, so both are captured fresh each render).
- **Schema tripwire (`test_schema.cjs` + `schema.expected.json`) ŌĆö the (ii) tooling.** Freezes the key-sets of `DEFAULT_G/D`, `SEG_DEFAULTS`, `DEF_SECTION`, `DEFAULT_LINE/PLACED` + `CURRENT_VERSION` + the `MIGRATIONS` step list. A rename/removal of a defaulted field (which flows silently through merge-on-defaults) makes the test FAIL and prints the migration ritual. Low-noise: it only fires on a deliberate shape change. (Verified it *bites*: a simulated `wWindŌåÆwindForce` rename is flagged removed+added.) **Limit it can't cover:** line geometry fields aren't in any default object, so a *geometry* rename isn't auto-caught ŌĆö that leans on the migration discipline + the stale fixture.
- **Migration-mechanism test (`test_migrate_ladder.cjs`).** `migrateProject(raw, migrations=MIGRATIONS, target=CURRENT_VERSION)` now takes injectable `migrations`/`target`, so a SYNTHETIC 3-step ladder proves the mechanism the real `MIGRATIONS[1]` (a no-op stamp) can't: steps run one-at-a-time **in order**, transform values **cumulatively** (`5 ŌåÆ ├Ś2 ŌåÆ +10 = 20`), stop at `target`, enter mid-ladder for a vN file, halt cleanly on a missing step, and compute `newer` against `target`. A worked **unit-conversion + rename template** is in the `MIGRATIONS` comment for when the first real breaking change lands.
- **Frozen fixtures.** `fixture_v1.wps` / `fixture_v2.wps` (from rev 23) are now treated as **frozen, hand-edited, never regenerated** (regenerating from new defaults after a migration would make a *fake* old file). Added `fixture_v2_design.wps` (a geometry-complete line + 2-segment layout ŌĆö exercises the lines/placed merge) and `fixture_v2_stale.wps` (one valid + one geometry-less line ŌĆö exercises the stale path + the keep-layout-by-id behavior).
- **Verification:** esbuild bundle clean ┬Ę comment-lexer clean ┬Ę render smoke PASS with the **plan-tab render byte-identical to baseline** (27041 chars) ┬Ę design + calc SSR-mount ┬Ę **stale banner renders in-context** (App on the Design tab with `designStale` forced true ŌåÆ banner copy + "Rebuild from plan" present) ┬Ę engine guard CLEAN (11/11) ┬Ę `test_loadstate.cjs` **46/46** (rev-23 cases + design-merge + stale-path + lengthFt:0/missing-id drop) ┬Ę `test_schema.cjs` **8/8 frozen** (+ a negative test confirming it detects a rename) ┬Ę `test_migrate_ladder.cjs` **12/12**.

### Migration checklist ŌĆö RUN THIS whenever you change the MEANING, UNIT, NAME, or PRESENCE of a saved field

merge-on-defaults (rev 23ŌĆō24) silently handles **added** fields. It does **NOT** handle renames, removals, or unit/semantics changes ŌĆö those load with *no error* and a *wrong value*. So, before shipping any such change:

1. **Bump `CURRENT_VERSION`** (e.g. 2 ŌåÆ 3).
2. **Add the `MIGRATIONS[oldV]` step** that transforms an old project into the new shape (rename the key, convert the unit, drop the obsolete field). Template is in the `MIGRATIONS` comment.
3. **Freeze a fixture at the OLD version** ŌĆö hand-author or copy an existing pre-change `.wps`; never regenerate it from new defaults.
4. **Add a load assertion** in `test_loadstate.cjs` that the OLD fixture loads to the NEW correct value (this is the *only* thing that catches a botched unit conversion ŌĆö the engine guard can't, it guards code not data interpretation).
5. **Update `schema.expected.json`** so `test_schema.cjs` goes green again (this is also the prompt that reminded you to do steps 1ŌĆō4).

## 4y. Rev 25 ŌĆö User-facing app version in the top bar (user-requested)

User asked for a version number at the top that reads "Version 1.00" and counts up 1.01, 1.02, ŌĆ” per update, rolling 1.99 ŌåÆ 2.00.

- **Two module-scope constants at the very top of the jsx** (placed first for discoverability, since they're bumped every release): `const APP_BUILD = 100;` (integer hundredths, the single thing you bump) and `const APP_VERSION = \`${Math.floor(APP_BUILD/100)}.${String(APP_BUILD%100).padStart(2,"0")}\`;` ŌåÆ `"1.00"`. Integer math (floor + `%` + `padStart`), so the rollover is correct **by construction**: 100ŌåÆ"1.00", 101ŌåÆ"1.01", 110ŌåÆ"1.10", 199ŌåÆ"1.99", 200ŌåÆ"2.00", 1099ŌåÆ"10.99" (all unit-tested).
- **Displayed** as `Version {APP_VERSION}` at the right end of the sticky suite tab bar (`marginLeft:"auto"` pushes it past the three tabs), in mono/`SW.faint` to match the drafting eyebrow type. It's inside the `no-print tbar`, so it shows on screen but not on printed calc sheets (offer to also stamp it into the calc/design title blocks if the user wants it on output ŌĆö deliberately NOT done here to avoid changing the calc sheet).
- **THREE independent version counters now exist ŌĆö do not couple them.** `APP_VERSION` (this, user-facing UI) ┬Ę `CURRENT_VERSION = 2` (save-file schema, drives `.wps` migrations) ┬Ę the handoff "rev" number (dev changelog). The header comment over `APP_BUILD` spells this out. Bumping the display version must never touch `CURRENT_VERSION`.
- **UI-only.** No engine/loader/schema/serialization touched: the byte-identity guard is CLEAN (11/11), and all three save-file suites (`test_loadstate` 46/46, `test_schema` 8/8, `test_migrate_ladder` 12/12) pass unchanged. `APP_BUILD`/`APP_VERSION` are intentionally NOT in `schema.expected.json` (they aren't save-file schema).
- **Verification:** esbuild bundle clean ┬Ę engine guard CLEAN ┬Ę version-format rollover 8/8 boundary cases ┬Ę render smoke shows "Version 1.00" in the top bar + all three tabs still present ┬Ę design + calc tabs SSR-mount ┬Ę save-file suites unaffected.



1. **South-wall 80 ft cap**: typed lengths extended from the lower-ID node and clamped at x=0 ŌåÆ world is now **symmetric ┬▒WORLD** at *all 6 clamp sites* (typed len ├Ś2, split, node drag ├Ś2, wall drag dx/dy).
2. **~80 ft drag reach**: frozen view capped gestures ŌåÆ `expandViewTo` live zoom-out.
3. **Design tab empty after handoff**: `buildSecData`'s reaction aggregation dropped `key` (`agg[rr.key]={kips,ax,ay}`) ŌåÆ now `{key:rr.key,...}`. Button finds edges by `r.key`.
