## 4z. Rev 26 ŌĆö TWO-STORY WOOD SHEAR WALL DESIGN (multi-step, in progress)

User-requested simple two-story option. **Model decision:** the two floors share ONE footprint + ONE shear-wall layout, so they are identical and vertically aligned by construction (no second graph to keep in sync; alignment for stacking is just "same segment index, same line"). Per-wall heights: existing `H`/`leeH` = 1st-story windward/leeward; new `H2`/`leeH2` = 2nd-story windward/leeward. **Engine invariant:** the 7 guarded fns (`calcSegment`, `generateDesign`, `evaluateCandidate`, `lineResults`, `withUtil`, `buildSecData`, `lineReactions`) stay byte-identical ŌĆö every new structural quantity is derived OUTSIDE them (the `withUtil` pattern). Built step-by-step, user previews each before the next.

**The structural model (confirmed with the user):**
- **Roof diaphragm line load** (designs the **2nd-floor** shear walls) = `┬Į┬ĘHŌéé┬Ępw + parapets`. Equivalently `buildSecData`'s 1-story `w.total` with HŌåÆHŌéé: `roofLL = w.total + ┬Į┬Ę(HŌééŌłÆH)┬Ępw` (parapets are height-independent so they cancel in the delta). Example: 374 + ┬Į(10ŌłÆ13)16 = **350 plf**.
- **2nd-floor diaphragm line load** (designs the **1st-floor** shear walls) = `┬Į┬ĘHŌéé┬Ępw + ┬Į┬ĘH┬Ępw + roofLL` (2nd-story wall's lower half + 1st-story wall's upper half + the whole roof load transferred down). Example: 80 + 104 + 350 = **534 plf**. The ┬Į┬ĘHŌéé┬Ępw appears in both loads but for DIFFERENT halves of the 2nd-story wall (upperŌåÆroof, lowerŌåÆ2nd-floor) ŌĆö not a double-count.
- **Vertical load stacking (Step 6, statics note ŌĆö IMPORTANT):** stacking is by **overturning moment with the correct arm**, NOT a flat sum of chord reactions. The roof reaction sits a full story higher, so at the 1st-floor base it acts at `HŌéü+HŌéé`. The user corrected the illustrative "11k = 6k+5k": e.g. roof 5k├Ś20ft + floor 6k├Ś10ft, over a 10ft wall = (100+60)/10 = **16k**. So Step 6 accumulates `╬ŻRßĄó┬ĘhßĄó` (hßĄó from this wall's base) and re-derives end-post/holdown from the combined moment ŌĆö done in a post-process wrapper, engine untouched.

**Step log (each = one preview-and-approve increment):**
- **Step 1 (build 101ŌåÆ102, UI scaffold).** App-level `twoStory`/`activeFloor` state (persisted in the `ui` slice, feature-detected on load; old files default to single-story; `CURRENT_VERSION` untouched). A **sliding 1-Story/2-Story pill** in a "Stories" ribbon group (`.storypill`/`.storythumb`/`.storyopt`, drafting blue, white thumb) ŌĆö replaced the first-cut button at the user's request (screenshot of a segmented toggle). Floor selector moved **out of the canvas into its own `.floorbar` below the stage** (was an absolute overlay; clicks were intercepted by the SVG pointer handlers ŌĆö the fix was to stop overlapping the canvas). `.canvascol` wraps the stage + floorbar.
- **Step 2 (build 103, data model).** `H2` added to `DEF_SECTION` (default `null`) and resolved in `mergeWallProps` (null ŌåÆ equals that wall's `H`), so toggling on changes nothing until edited; old files + new walls resolve correctly; legacy `parW`ŌåÆ`par` still migrates; the line-load inputs `buildSecData` reads are unchanged. `H2` rides in `wallProps` so save/load round-trips for free. A "Floor N" badge (pointer-events:none) marks the canvas in 2-story mode.
- **Step 3 (build 104, the two line loads).** Formulas above computed in the wind window (UI, outside the engine) and shown as a two-value readout (roof ŌåÆ 2nd-floor walls; 2nd-floor ŌåÆ 1st-floor walls) with itemized components, live as `HŌéé` is edited. 1-story mode shows the original single "Total wall line load". Degenerate `HŌéé=H` falls back to the familiar 1-story number (no surprise on toggle).
- **Step 4 (build 105ŌåÆ106, section-cut graphics).** New `SecDiagram2` component (sibling to `SecDiagram`, which is left byte-identical) draws the stacked two-story elevation: parapets, 2nd story (HŌéé) + 1st story (H) split by a dashed 2nd-floor diaphragm line, windward wall pressure over both stories, leeward parapet pressure, gold callouts labeling both diaphragm line loads, "1st floor ┬Ę foundation" base. The Step-2 stopgap `H2` text field was removed (the diagram's red box is now the editor). **Leeward parity (build 106, user-requested):** the two-story diagram shows its own leeward 1st/2nd-story heights (`leeH`/`leeH2`) on the right, editable, exactly like the single-story diagram's leeward height ŌĆö roof and 2nd-floor lines slope if windwardŌēĀleeward. `leeH2` forwarded via `activeSection`, seeded in the window, routed in `upd` (`prop==="leeH2"` ŌåÆ `setVals("lee",{H2})`). Leeward heights are display-only for the loads (which use the windward side).
- **Step 5 ŌĆö part 1 (build 107, on-plan loads go floor-aware; user report: "loads on the plan don't change when I switch floors").** `propsForActive` wraps `propsFor` with a floor-specific EFFECTIVE wall height and feeds it to the `secH`/`secV` `buildSecData` calls (engine reads `pr.H` ONLY in the line-load term ŌĆö verified ŌĆö so the substitution scales line loads AND reactions with no geometric distortion): 2nd-floor plan ŌåÆ `H_eff = HŌéé` (roof diaphragm, 350-level); 1st-floor plan ŌåÆ `H_eff = H + 2┬ĘHŌéé` (2nd-floor diaphragm, 534-level; `┬Į(H+2HŌéé)pw = ┬ĮH┬Ępw + HŌéé┬Ępw`, parapets ride along height-independently). 1-story mode passes through unchanged (byte-identical). Now the on-plan plf labels, reactions, and base shear all reflect the selected floor.
- **Step 5 ŌĆö part 2 (build 108, both floors designed + Design-tab switcher).** `runDesignHandoff` now builds BOTH floors' lines in 2-story mode (`buildFloor(2)` from roof reactions @ design height `HŌéé`; `buildFloor(1)` from 2nd-floor reactions @ design height `H` ŌĆö the `heightFt` is now floor-correct, previously always `H`) by re-running the frozen `buildSecData` with each floor's effective-height props. Handoff payload changed `lines` ŌåÆ `byFloor = {1:[ŌĆ”],2:[ŌĆ”]}`. App stores `designLinesByFloor`; `designLines` is now a DERIVED memo (`designLinesByFloor[activeFloor]`) so the Design tab + everything downstream is unchanged. `segsByLine` is SHARED across floors (shear walls are vertically aligned ŌåÆ same positions; only the per-floor forces/heights differ, so the auto-design results differ per floor). A **floor switcher** ("Designing 1st/2nd Floor") sits in the Design-tab constraints header, greyed until 2-story, and sets `activeFloor` (synced with the plan selector ŌĆö one "current floor" concept). Switching floors re-derives the active lines with no recompute of the wind analysis. **Save/load:** `design.linesByFloor` (canonical); `loadProject` accepts either the new object OR a legacy `design.lines` array (ŌåÆ `{1:[ŌĆ”]}`), validates each floor's geometry, and keeps the stale-recovery flag. KNOWN LIMITATION (acceptable for now, flagged to user): per-segment manual overrides (holdown/nailing/post) in `segsByLine` are shared across floors; the AUTO design already differs per floor.

**New/changed identifiers:** state `twoStory`,`activeFloor` (App) ┬Ę `propsForActive` (floor-specific effective height) ┬Ę `designLinesByFloor` (per-floor design store; `designLines` now derived) ┬Ę `DEF_SECTION.H2` ┬Ę `mergeWallProps` H2 resolution ┬Ę `activeSection.{H2,leeH2}` ┬Ę WindWindow `roofLL`/`floorLL`/`wallRes2` + `twoStory` prop + `leeH2` seed/route ┬Ę `SecDiagram2` ┬Ę CSS `.storypill/.storythumb/.storyopt/.canvascol/.floorbar/.floorsel/.floortab/.floorbadge` (and now-unused `.h2row*`).

**Verification each step:** esbuild compile + comment-balance + cjs bundle ┬Ę App render smoke (1-story default unchanged, version ticks) ┬Ę focused `SecDiagram2` render via a throwaway temp-export copy (callouts 350/534, four height boxes, sloped case no-NaN) ┬Ę headless formula test (350/534 + degenerate) ┬Ę headless `mergeWallProps` test (H2 resolution + backward-compat) ┬Ę **engine byte-identity guard CLEAN every step**. (The original `.mjs`/`.cjs` harness files from ┬¦6/┬¦6b were not in this session's zip; the substantive protections ŌĆö engine guard + targeted headless tests ŌĆö were reproduced inline. Step 7 will re-establish the checked-in fixtures + schema tripwire for the added fields.)

## 4aa. Rev 27 ŌĆö Step 6: arm-aware vertical load stacking (1st-floor overturning)

The 1st-floor shear walls now resist the upper story's overturning with the **correct moment arm**. This is the one structurally substantive step of the two-story feature, and it lands **without touching the engine** ŌĆö the 7 guarded fns (`calcSegment`, `generateDesign`, `evaluateCandidate`, `lineResults`, `withUtil`, `buildSecData`, `lineReactions`) are byte-identical (engine guard CLEAN), exactly like Steps 1ŌĆō5. All new logic is a post-process wrapper, the `withUtil` pattern.

- **The statics (clean result).** Stacking is by **overturning moment with the right arm**, not a flat sum of chord reactions. The roof reaction sits a full upper story higher, so at the 1st-floor base it acts at `HŌéü+HŌéé`. Because **Step 5 already gave each floor the correct force AND design height** (1st floor = combined 534-level reaction @ `H`; 2nd floor = roof reaction @ `HŌéé`), the arm-aware base moment is **exactly the sum of the two floors' engine overturning moments for the same vertically-aligned segment**: `M_base = MotW(1st) + MotW(2nd)` (and likewise seismic). Worked: roof 5k @ 20ft + 2nd-floor 6k @ 10ft over a 10ft wall ŌåÆ MotW(1st)=11k┬Ę10=110, MotW(2nd)=5k┬Ę10=50, sum **160 k┬Ęft** ŌåÆ `T = 160000/(LŌłÆ0.125) Ōēł 16,203 lbs` (the user's "16k, not 11k"). The reason the sum works: the 1st-floor `forceLbs` is the combined reaction (incl. the roof transferred down), and its engine moment already counts the WHOLE combined shear at arm `HŌéü`; adding the 2nd-floor engine moment (roof shear at arm `HŌéé`) supplies exactly the missing `R_roof┬ĘHŌéé` so the roof's effective arm becomes `HŌéü+HŌéé`. No new arm bookkeeping needed.
- **Where it lives.** Three new module-level helpers next to `lineResults` (NOT inside it): `upliftStk` (mirror of `calcSegment`'s local `upliftFn`), `stackSeg(r1, r2, L, hdDist, thickness, isWood)` (combines the two floors' `MotW`/`MotS`, then recomputes `compW`/`compS`/`upHD_*`/`maxComp`/`maxUplift` and re-runs the engine's **own** end-post ladder + `HD_TABLE` lookup from `r1.Pa`/`r1.wdl`/`r1.AwDL`/`r1.CwDL`/`r1.BwDL`), and `stackedLineResults(line1, line2, segs, g, d)` (runs `lineResults` for BOTH floors on the shared segments, stacks per segment, then re-derives `ovBad`/`dispHd`/`dispPost`/`failed` from the stacked numbers). All of these reuse the existing `xMax`/`HD_TABLE`/`postAllowable`/`hdCapacity` ŌĆö no engine code copied that isn't a pure formula shape.
- **Wiring.** `DesignTab` gained a `linesByFloor` prop (App passes `designLinesByFloor`); its `resultsByLine` memo now stacks **only when `twoStory && activeFloor===1`** by matching each 1st-floor line to its 2nd-floor twin via the shared `id` (`ax|key`) and shared `segsByLine[id]`. The 2nd-floor view and 1-story mode keep calling plain `lineResults` (byte-identical behavior). The stacked results flow into BOTH the on-plan holdown bubbles and the selected-line table for free (single source).
- **What shear is NOT.** Stacking changes **only overturning** (post/holdown). The in-plane **shear/nailing** were already correct from Step 5 (the 534-level load carries the combined shear), so `status`/`selType`/`vW`/`vS`/`autoType` pass through unchanged ŌĆö verified in the test (`stk.vW === r1.vW`, `stk.selType === r1.selType`).
- **UI.** When viewing the 1st floor in 2-story mode the selected-line table shows (a) a blue **note** explaining the arm-aware stacking and listing what is/isn't stacked, and (b) a new **"Overturning M ┬Ę stacked"** row (governing `max(MotW,MotS)` in k┬Ęft, accent-colored). Both are gated on `stacking` and absent on the 2nd floor / 1-story.
- **Scope note (flagged to the user + in the UI).** End post + max uplift + holdown are stacked; **anchor / strap / deflection / footing rows still reflect the single-floor 1st-story demand.** Those are secondary detailing keyed off the holdown; wiring them to the stacked uplift means mirroring `calcSegment`'s `anchorFor`/`embedFor`/`strapFor`/deflection/footing math outside the engine (Ōēł40+ branchy lines). **User-confirmed (rev 27 session): do this together in Step 7** ŌĆö i.e. Step 7 bundles (a) anchor/strap/footing/deflection re-derived from the stacked uplift/moment with (b) persistence/regression/finalize. A stacked holdown that reads `NG!` (uplift > HDU14 cap) correctly signals the demand even while the anchor row is unstacked, so the interim state is safe to test on the live deploy.
- **Verification:** esbuild compile + comment-lexer clean ┬Ę engine guard CLEAN (7 fns byte-identical vs the session baseline) ┬Ę App render smoke OK ┬Ę new `work/test_stacking.cjs` (12 asserts: `MotW(stk)=MotW1+MotW2`; the 160 k┬Ęft / ~16,203-lb example; uplift > single-floor; single-floor `HDU14` vs stacked `NG!`; shear/selType unchanged; 2nd-floor carries no `stacked` flag) ┬Ę new `work/test_design_2story_ssr.cjs` (7 asserts: stacking note + overturning row + `160.0` render on the 1st floor; both absent on the 2nd). **New identifiers:** `upliftStk`, `stackSeg`, `stackedLineResults` ┬Ę `DesignTab` prop `linesByFloor` ┬Ę `resultsByLine` `stacking` flag ┬Ę table "Overturning M ┬Ę stacked" row + note. `APP_BUILD = 109` ("Version 1.09").

## 4bb. Rev 28 ŌĆö Step 7a/7c: secondary detailing wired to the stacked demand + regression lock

Step 6 stacked only the **primary** overturning items (end post + uplift + holdown). Step 7a finishes the 1st-floor design by re-deriving the **secondary detailing** from the SAME arm-aware combined moment, so a stacked 1st-floor line is now internally consistent end-to-end. As with Steps 1ŌĆō6, **the 7 guarded engine fns are byte-identical (guard CLEAN)** ŌĆö every new quantity is a formula-shape mirror living in the `stackSeg` wrapper, never in `calcSegment`/`lineResults`.

- **What's now stacked (added in 7a).** Inside `stackSeg`: **anchor** `anchorSel`/`anchorEnd` (mirror of `calcSegment.anchorFor`, keyed off the stacked `hd`/`maxUplift` + `d.anchor`), **embedment** `embed`/`embedEnd` (mirror of `embedFor`), **straps** `altStrap`/`strapCorner` (mirror of `strapFor`, driven by a new stacked `upStrap_W`/`upStrap_S`/`maxStrap` computed with the E56/E57 **denominator of 3ŌĆ│** ŌĆö distinct from the holdown denominator `1.5+hdDist`), **deflection** `deflW`/`deflS` (mirror of `defl`), and **footing** `reqFtgLen`/`LminS`/`LminW` (mirror of the `quad` + `P65`/`P70` footing block). Combined with the Step-6 `MotW`/`MotS`/`compW`/`compS`/`upHD_*`/`post`/`hd`, the stacked return object now overrides every detailing field.
- **Signature change.** `stackSeg(r1, r2, L, hdDist, thickness, isWood)` ŌåÆ **`stackSeg(r1, r2, L, g, d, h)`**. It now derives `sp`/`SCHED` from `g`, `anchor`/`hdDist`/`thickness`/`ftgWidth`/`ftgThick` from `d`, and takes the design height `h` (= `line1.heightFt`, for the deflection term). `stackedLineResults` passes `line1.heightFt`. No other call sites.
- **Dead-load + shear convention (kept from Step 6).** The stacked footing/uplift/compression use the **1st-floor's own** `wdl`/`B`/`BwDL`/`CwDL`/`AwDL` and base shear `Fs`/`Fw` (`r1.*`) with the **summed** moments. This matches Step 6's choice (combined moment + 1st-floor stabilizing dead load; conservative for uplift). If a future step wants the upper story's tributary dead load to add stabilizing weight at the 1st-floor base, that's a deliberate change to revisit with the user ŌĆö not done here.
- **Deflection subtlety (flagged in the UI).** `v` (`r1.vW`/`r1.vS`) is unchanged ŌĆö the 1st-floor story shear was already the combined 534-level shear from Step 5. Only the bending term's chord area uses the **stacked** end post. Since stacking only adds moment, the stacked post is Ōēź the single-floor post, so the stacked ╬ö is Ōēż the single-floor ╬ö (monotone). The Design-tab note explains this so a smaller stacked ╬ö isn't read as an error.
- **UI.** The blue stacking note in the selected-line table was rewritten: it no longer claims anchor/strap/deflection/footing are unstacked; it now says every row reflects the stacked demand and explains the ╬ö-with-stiffer-post behavior. The "Overturning M ┬Ę stacked" row is unchanged.
- **Calc-sheet interaction (unchanged).** `applyToCalc` ("Send line to calculation sheet") still forwards only geometry + `selType` + `forceLbs`; the Calculation tab recomputes via `calcSegment` and is a single-line/single-floor view with NO moment stacking. Stacking is a Design-tab-only concept (`resultsByLine`). Documented so nobody "fixes" the calc sheet to stack.
- **Verification:** esbuild compile + comment-lexer balanced (72/72) ┬Ę engine guard CLEAN (7 fns byte-identical vs the session baseline) ┬Ę App render smoke 6/6 ┬Ę engine golden 22/22 unchanged ┬Ę note text confirmed in the built bundle (new note present, old caveat removed) ┬Ę new checked-in `work/test_stacking_step7.cjs` (**25 asserts**): (A) ┬¦4aa 160 k┬Ęft / ~16,203-lb example + NG! holdown + shear/selType unchanged; (B) exact discrete buckets on a 5000-lb stacked uplift ŌåÆ `HDU5` ŌåÆ anchor `SSTB24` ŌåÆ embed `Simpson`, strap uplift 5064.1 lbs (denom 3) ŌåÆ `altStrap STHD14` / `strapCorner None`, deflection finite>0, footing Ōēź L+1; (C) end-to-end via `stackedLineResults` with real engine floors ŌåÆ moment = sum, uplift/comp/footing Ōēź single-floor, ╬ö Ōēż single-floor, shear/selType unchanged, valid anchor string, 1st-floor `stacked` flag set, top floor (no twin) NOT stacked. **New identifiers:** `stackSeg` stacked fields `upStrap_W`/`upStrap_S`/`maxStrap`/`anchorSel`/`anchorEnd`/`embed`/`embedEnd`/`altStrap`/`strapCorner`/`deflW`/`deflS`/`LminS`/`LminW`/`reqFtgLen`. `APP_BUILD = 110` ("Version 1.10").

## 4cc. Rev 28 ŌĆö Step 7b: two-story persistence regression lock (fixtures + round-trip + schema tripwire)

The final Step-7 sub-task. It re-establishes the ┬¦4w/┬¦4x save-file protections, now extended to cover the two-story fields, and proves a two-story project survives a `.wps` save/open. **No app code changed** ŌĆö the persistence already worked end-to-end (it was built incrementally in Steps 1ŌĆō5); 7b is checked-in test/fixture infrastructure that LOCKS it. The jsx stays at build 110.

- **Why it's testable without App surgery.** `loadProject`, `migrateProject`, and `mergeWallProps` are all **module-level pure functions** (not React closures): `loadProject(raw)` returns ready-to-dispatch slices and the `onFileChosen` handler just dispatches them. So the `work/exp.cjs` save/load-core bundle the older handoff referenced is rebuilt by appending one export line and esbuild-bundling (`export { loadProject, migrateProject, mergeWallProps, MIGRATIONS, CURRENT_VERSION, DEF_SECTION, DEFAULT_G, DEFAULT_D, SEG_DEFAULTS, DEFAULT_LINE, DEFAULT_PLACED };`).
- **How two-story state persists (confirmed by the test).** `H2` rides inside `sketcher.wallProps[key].H2` (restored verbatim by `projectRef.current.set`, then resolved at render by `mergeWallProps`: explicit value kept, `null` ŌåÆ that wall's `H`). The per-floor design is `design.linesByFloor` `{1:[ŌĆ”],2:[ŌĆ”]}` (loader normalizes a legacy single `design.lines` array ŌåÆ `{1:[ŌĆ”]}`). Mode is `ui.twoStory` / `ui.activeFloor` (old files lack them ŌåÆ `false` / `1`). The save `proj` shape (`onSave`): `{ app, version:2, savedAt, sketcher, design:{ linesByFloor, shape, segsByLine, d, selLine }, calc:{ g, segments }, ui:{ tab, hlSel, twoStory, activeFloor } }`.
- **Fixture.** `work/fixtures/fixture_v2_2story.wps` ŌĆö a hand-built v2 two-story project matching that exact `onSave` shape: a 40├Ś24 plan, two `wallProps` entries (one `H2:10`, one `H2:null`), `linesByFloor` floors 1 (combined `forceLbs` 16000) and 2 (roof 7000) sharing line id `h|A` and `segsByLine`, full `d`/`g`/`segments`, `ui.twoStory:true`.
- **Round-trip test.** `work/test_loadstate_2story.cjs` (**31 asserts**): (A) the fixture loads with `twoStory`/`activeFloor`/`tab` restored, both floors' lines kept (no false stale drop), geometry + per-floor forces preserved, shared `segsByLine` intact, `g`/`d`/`segments` merged onto defaults, `sketcher.wallProps` preserved verbatim; (B) `mergeWallProps` resolves `H2` (explicit kept, `null`ŌåÆ`H`, missing propsŌåÆdefault `H`, legacy `parW`ŌåÆ`par`); (C) v1 back-compat (no `ui`, single `design.lines` array ŌåÆ `linesByFloor[1]`, defaults applied, migrates to v2); (D) a `version:99` file sets `newer:true`; (E) stale-line recovery (a geometry-less line is dropped + `stale` raised, its `segsByLine` entry KEPT for rebuild, two-story `ui` still restored).
- **Schema tripwire.** `work/test_schema.cjs` + `work/fixtures/schema.expected.json` (**15 asserts**) re-derive the live key-sets of `DEF_SECTION`/`DEFAULT_G`/`DEFAULT_D`/`SEG_DEFAULTS`/`DEFAULT_LINE`/`DEFAULT_PLACED` and the `loadProject` output `ui`/`design`/`calc` shapes, compare to the frozen expected, and FAIL on any add/remove/rename ŌĆö plus hardcoded presence checks for `H2`/`twoStory`/`activeFloor`/`linesByFloor` that survive a careless expected-file regen. **Verified to fire** on a simulated `H2`ŌåÆ`h2` rename (negative control). This is the guard that forces a future rename to ship with a `CURRENT_VERSION` bump + a `MIGRATIONS` step + a fixture ŌĆö merge-on-defaults silently mis-loads renamed fields, so without this they'd pass unnoticed. **Caveat (unchanged from ┬¦4x):** line GEOMETRY-field renames (`id`/`a`/`b`/`lengthFt` ŌĆö not in a default object) are NOT auto-caught; they rely on discipline.
- **Save-file status:** still no real `.wps` files in the wild (Save-Open hasn't been used in anger ŌĆö the app is deployed as of rev 29, but no real save has been made yet), so 7b is pre-emptive insurance. If a breaking schema change ever lands, freeze a fixture at the OLD version and add a load-assertion (the migration checklist in ┬¦4x / ┬¦7). **New checked-in artifacts:** `work/exp.cjs`, `work/fixtures/fixture_v2_2story.wps`, `work/fixtures/schema.expected.json`, `work/test_loadstate_2story.cjs`, `work/test_schema.cjs` (+ the rev-28a `work/sw_stack.cjs`, `work/test_stacking_step7.cjs`). No app change; `APP_BUILD = 110`.






## 4dd. Rev 29 ŌĆö Deployed to Vercel (Vite host scaffold; NO app-code change)

The app went live on Vercel. The single-file React component is byte-identical ŌĆö a thin Vite host shell was added AROUND it so a static build can mount it. **`APP_BUILD` stays 110 ("Version 1.10"); engine + the 7 guarded fns untouched; the jsx was not edited.** This is an infrastructure rev, so there is no version bump (the version display tracks app-code changes, and there were none).

- **The deployable repo (FLAT layout ŌĆö all files at root).** The delivered zip is the source of truth:
  ```
  (repo root)
  Ōö£ŌöĆ index.html                 ŌåÉ Vite entry
  Ōö£ŌöĆ main.jsx                   ŌåÉ mounts <App/>
  Ōö£ŌöĆ plan-sketcher-suite.jsx    ŌåÉ the app, UNCHANGED
  Ōö£ŌöĆ package.json
  Ōö£ŌöĆ vite.config.js
  Ōö£ŌöĆ .gitignore
  ŌööŌöĆ PLAN_SKETCHER_SUITE_HANDOFF.md   ŌåÉ this file (added rev 29)
  ```
  **ŌÜĀ Layout note:** the rev-29 chat *prose* described a `src/`-nested layout (`src/main.jsx`, `src/plan-sketcher-suite.jsx`). The actual delivered files are FLAT ŌĆö `index.html` loads `./main.jsx`, and `main.jsx` imports `./plan-sketcher-suite.jsx`, both root-relative. If you re-issue the scaffold, match the flat layout that's live (or move both into `src/` AND update the two relative import paths together ŌĆö don't half-do it).
- **`index.html`** ŌĆö `#root` div + `<script type="module" src="./main.jsx">`. Carries a **4-line host reset**: `html,body{margin:0;padding:0}` + `#root{min-height:100vh}`. Reason: the app injects all its own styling but never resets the default body margin, and its roots size to `calc(100vh ŌłÆ 46px)` ŌĆö without the reset you get a gutter. **This reset lives in the SHELL, not in the app file** (keeps the app byte-identical and portable).
- **`main.jsx`** ŌĆö `import React from "react"` + `import ReactDOM from "react-dom/client"` + `import App from "./plan-sketcher-suite.jsx"`; `createRoot(#root).render(<React.StrictMode><App/></React.StrictMode>)`. The app's `export default function App()` is exactly what this expects.
- **`package.json`** ŌĆö `"version":"1.10.0"`, `"type":"module"`; deps `react`/`react-dom` `^18.3.1`; devDeps `vite ^5.4.10` + `@vitejs/plugin-react ^4.3.4`; scripts `dev`/`build`/`preview`.
- **`vite.config.js`** ŌĆö just `react()` plugin.
- **`.gitignore`** ŌĆö `node_modules`, `dist`, `dist-ssr`, `.DS_Store`, `*.local`, `.vercel`, `npm-debug.log*`.
- **Why a bare mount suffices (re-verified against the source).** The only real `import` is `react` (the `ŌĆ”xlsx` grep hits are all inside comments, lines ~1962/1968/1969). No CSS-file imports (styling = injected `<style>` strings; IBM Plex from Google Fonts at runtime). No `import.meta`, no `process.env`, no `ReactDOM` inside the app file. So the shell's whole job is: provide React + react-dom and mount `<App/>`.
- **No `vercel.json`.** Navigation is internal tab state (no react-router / no URL routes) ŌåÆ nothing to rewrite, no SPA-fallback rule needed.
- **Vercel project settings (auto-detected Vite, no overrides):** Framework Preset **Vite** ┬Ę Build `npm run build` ┬Ę Output `dist` ┬Ę Install `npm install`. Every push to `main` auto-redeploys.
- **Handoff-in-repo:** the first push omitted this MD; rev 29 adds it to the repo so the handoff travels with the code (per the ┬¦0 "handoff tracks code" rule, now also "handoff ships in the repo").
- **OPEN ŌĆö the one live sign-off (unchanged target, now actionable on the live URL):** preview the stacked 1st-floor detailing and a two-story `.wps` save/open on the deployed Vercel site, then sign off to close the Step-7 two-story feature.

## 4ee. Rev 30 ŌĆö Text Scale control on the Plan Sketcher toolbar (user-requested)

**The problem.** On-plan label text is sized `fontSize = 1.35┬ĘS`, where `S = Math.max(view.w, view.h)/110` (line ~1004). `S` grows as you zoom out (the viewBox widens), which keeps the label at a roughly **constant screen size** at any zoom. Great for a normal plan; bad for a large plan zoomed way out ŌĆö the building shrinks but the labels don't, so they blanket the drawing. The user asked for a scaler to shrink them.

**The control.** A new ribbon group **Text** (a `<div className="rgroup">` with `rlabel` "Text"), placed **between View and Stories**, holding a single `<select className="rsel">` with options `1├Ś` / `0.75├Ś` / `0.5├Ś` / `0.25├Ś` (default `1├Ś`). `value={textScale} onChange={e=>setTextScale(parseFloat(e.target.value))}` ŌĆö state stays numeric so the components can multiply by it directly. New CSS class `.rsel` (added right after `.rbtn:disabled`) mirrors `.rbtn`'s look (white, ink, hoverŌåÆaccent, focus ring); it is a native select so it's keyboard/AX-friendly and needs no popover code.

**State.** `const [textScale,setTextScale]=useState(1);` declared in `PlanSketcher` immediately after `dims` (line ~911). Default `1` ŌćÆ no behavioral change from rev 29.

**Where it applies (the COMPLETE set of sketcher-canvas text ŌĆö nothing in the wind-window modal / `SecDiagram*`, which are fixed-size in their own panel):**
- `Tag({ŌĆ”, ts=1})` ŌĆö used by **dimension labels** and the **reaction rocket chip**. Scales `fs=1.35┬ĘS┬Ęts` AND the box (`w` padding term, `h` via fs, `rx`, the text y-nudge) so the whole chip shrinks, not just the glyphs (a shrunk glyph in a full-size box wouldn't reduce obstruction).
- `WindLoad({ŌĆ”, ts=1})` ŌĆö the `ŌĆ” plf` label (`fontSize={1.35*S*ts}`). Arrows/lines/offsets unchanged.
- `Reaction({ŌĆ”, ts=1})` ŌĆö threads `ts` straight into its `<Tag ŌĆ” ts={ts}/>`.
- Two inline canvas texts in `PlanSketcher`: the **draw-mode live length** `{L}ŌĆ▓` and the **`ŌÜĀ imbalance`** flag ŌĆö each multiplied by `*textScale`.
- Mount sites pass `ts={textScale}`: `<WindLoad ŌĆ”>` (├Ś2, h/v), `<Reaction ŌĆ”>` (├Ś2), and the dimension `<Tag ŌĆ”>`.

**`ts` defaults to 1 on every component**, so all pre-existing call sites (and the SSR smokes, and any future re-use) render byte-identically. Only text size + the `Tag` box that wraps text respond to the control; **no drawing geometry** (strokes, arrows, nodes, grid, divides, box *positions*) moves.

**Persistence.** `textScale` is added to the sketcher session `get()` snapshot (`ŌĆ”, dims, textScale }`) and restored in `set()` via `if("textScale" in s) setTextScale(Number(s.textScale)||1);` ŌĆö forward-compatible (old `.wps` lacking the field default to `1`). **This is sketcher session-UI, not part of `loadProject`'s `ui`/`design`/`calc` shapes, so the schema tripwire (`test_schema.cjs`) is unaffected** ŌĆö no `schema.expected.json` regen needed.

**Engine guard CLEAN.** All app-code changes are in: the `APP_BUILD` const, the `CSS` template (`.rsel`), the three module-scope sketcher visuals (`Tag`/`WindLoad`/`Reaction`), and `PlanSketcher` (state + ribbon JSX + two inline texts + session get/set). The engine and the 10 engine/stacking functions verified this rev (`calcSegment`, `generateDesign`, `lineReactions`, `buildSecData`, `findLeewardPartner`, `lineResults`, `stackSeg`, `stackedLineResults`, `upliftStk`, `withUtil` ŌĆö a superset of the canonical "7 guarded fns") are byte-identical ŌĆö verified by extract-and-diff against `.engine-baseline.jsx` (all 10 IDENTICAL).

**Verification.** esbuild compile OK; comment-lexer clean; SSR render smoke (asserts the **Text** group, all four options, default value 1, and that the **View** Fit button + **Stories** pill survive); focused component test exporting `Tag`/`Reaction`: `Tag` fontSize `13.5ŌåÆ6.75` at `ts .5`, box `width` shrinks, **omitted-`ts` ŌēĪ `ts:1`**, `Reaction` label `3.375` at `ts .25`. Render length 30,940 ŌåÆ 31,769 (the added dropdown). Build `APP_BUILD = 111` ("Version 1.11").

**Judgment call (reversible).** The draw-mode **live length** readout also obeys `textScale`, so at `0.25├Ś` it gets small while drawing. Included for consistency (it's on-plan text like the rest); exempting it is a one-line change (drop `*textScale` on that single inline `<text>`) if the user prefers it always full-size.

## 4ff. Rev 31 ŌĆö Plan glyphs halved: nodes, point-load arrow, plf line-load arrows (user-requested)

The user asked to halve three on-plan drawing elements (distinct from rev 30, which scaled *text*; this scales *glyphs/geometry*). All three derive their size from `S = Math.max(view.w,view.h)/110`, so each change is a literal-multiplier halving with a `rev 31:` inline comment for find/revert. **No state, no control** ŌĆö the user asked for a definite "half the size," not an adjustable knob.

- **(1) Wall nodes** ŌĆö the `graph.nodes.map(p=>ŌĆ”)` block in `PlanSketcher`:
  - visible dot `r={(isSel?1.05:0.85)*S}` ŌåÆ `r={(isSel?0.525:0.425)*S}`
  - selection halo `r={1.8*S}` ŌåÆ `r={0.9*S}` (kept proportional to the smaller dot)
  - dot stroke `strokeWidth={0.25*S}` ŌåÆ `{0.125*S}`
  - **the transparent hit-target `r={3.5*S}` is intentionally NOT halved** ŌĆö it's the click/right-click/grab target; shrinking it would hurt usability. (A comment marks it.)
- **(2) Point-load (reaction) arrow** ŌĆö `Reaction` (module scope):
  - `shaft = 2.1*S` ŌåÆ `1.05*S`
  - line `strokeWidth={0.42*S}` ŌåÆ `{0.21*S}`
  - the `#reactArr` arrowhead **auto-halves**: the marker has no `markerUnits`, so it defaults to `strokeWidth` and scales with the halved stroke. The kips label (`<Tag>`) is text ŌĆö untouched here (sized by rev-30 `ts`); with the shorter shaft it simply sits closer to the node.
- **(3) plf line-load arrows** ŌĆö `WindLoad` (module scope):
  - standoff/length `aLen = clamp(total/55,3,8)*0.5*S` ŌåÆ `*0.25*S`
  - `tip = 0.3*S` ŌåÆ `0.15*S` (so the drawn arrow shaft, `aLenŌłÆtip`, also halves)
  - baseline `strokeWidth={0.2*S}` ŌåÆ `{0.1*S}`; arrow `strokeWidth={0.16*S}` ŌåÆ `{0.08*S}` (the `#loadArr` arrowhead auto-halves with the stroke)
  - **untouched on purpose:** the arrow COUNT `n = max(2, round(len/(5.5*S)))` (density, not size ŌĆö the user wanted smaller arrows, not fewer) and the `ŌĆ” plf` label offset `aLen+2.2*S` (text; it follows the smaller `aLen` inward, which is fine).

**Not touched (scope discipline):** the draw-mode ghost node (`r={0.8*S}`) and the node-snap ring (`r={1.5*S}`) are transient drawing aids, not "the nodes," so they were left as-is. If the user notices the draw-preview dot looks bigger than the placed node, halving that one `0.8*S` is a trivial follow-up.

**Engine guard CLEAN.** The whole diff vs `.engine-baseline.jsx` is the `APP_BUILD` bump + exactly 7 visual lines (3 node, 2 `Reaction`, 4 `WindLoad` constants across 2 lines for stroke/aLen/tip). All 10 engine/stacking fns extract-and-diff IDENTICAL. **Verification:** esbuild compile OK; SSR render smoke (App mounts, nodes present); focused export test of `Reaction`/`WindLoad` confirms the halved stroke widths render (`Reaction` 4.2ŌåÆ2.1; `WindLoad` baseline 2ŌåÆ1, arrows 1.6ŌåÆ0.8) and the pre-halve values are gone. Build `APP_BUILD = 112` ("Version 1.12").

**If the user wants a different size later:** the knobs are the seven `rev 31:`-commented lines. Promoting them to one module-level constant (e.g. `const PLAN_GLYPH = 0.5;` multiplied into each) ŌĆö or a toolbar control mirroring the rev-30 Text dropdown ŌĆö is the natural next step *if and only if* they ask for adjustability; until then, literals keep it simple.

> **SUPERSEDED by rev 32 (┬¦4gg):** the user chose exactly that "toolbar control" path ŌĆö rev 32 reverted this hard-halving and folded nodes + arrows into the rev-30 dropdown as one unified scale. ┬¦4ff is retained as change-log history; the live behavior is in ┬¦4gg.

## 4gg. Rev 32 ŌĆö Unified "Markup" scale: text + arrows + nodes on one dropdown (user-requested)

**The decision.** After rev 31, the user said the arrows/nodes should be **scalable together with the text**, at original base size ŌĆö i.e. merge rev 30 (text scaler) and rev 31 (arrow/node size) into ONE control. So rev 32 reverts rev 31's hardcoded halving and makes the single dropdown scale the whole on-plan markup layer.

- **Revert + scale (base literals restored, then ├Ś the scale factor):**
  - **Nodes** (`graph.nodes.map`, `markScale` in scope): dot `(isSel?1.05:0.85)*S*markScale`, halo `1.8*S*markScale`, stroke `0.25*S*markScale`. The transparent **hit-target stays `3.5*S` (unscaled)** so a node shrunk to `0.25├Ś` is still easy to click/grab. Also the **draw-mode ghost-node preview** `0.8*S*markScale` (rev 31 had left it; now it tracks so the preview matches the placed node). Snap ring `1.5*S` left unscaled (osnap affordance).
  - **Reaction** (point-load arrow, prop `ts`): `shaft=2.1*S*ts`, stroke `0.42*S*ts`, label gap `1.55*S*ts` (so arrow + gap + label chip scale as one rocket).
  - **WindLoad** (plf arrows, prop `ts`): `aLen = clamp(ŌĆ”)*0.5*S*ts`, `tip=0.3*S*ts`, baseline stroke `0.2*S*ts`, arrow stroke `0.16*S*ts`, label gap `2.2*S*ts`. The arrow **COUNT** `n=max(2,round(len/(5.5*S)))` is deliberately NOT scaled ŌĆö scale changes glyph size, not density.
  - Arrowheads (`#reactArr`, `#loadArr`) auto-scale with their now-scaled stroke (markers default to `markerUnits="strokeWidth"`).
- **`ts` is the scale factor.** `Reaction`/`WindLoad`/`Tag` already received `ts={markScale}` (rev 30, for text); rev 32 simply multiplies `ts` into their geometry as well. Default `ts=1` ŌćÆ original size, so any other caller / DesignPlan reuse is unaffected.
- **Renames (UI + state):**
  - Ribbon group label **"Text" ŌåÆ "Markup"**; options changed from `Text 1├Ś`ŌĆ” to bare `1├Ś` / `0.75├Ś` / `0.5├Ś` / `0.25├Ś`; tooltip rewritten ("ŌĆ”shrink the labels, the load/reaction arrows, AND the nodes togetherŌĆ”").
  - State **`textScale` ŌåÆ `markScale`** / `setMarkScale`. Persisted in the `.wps` sketcher session under `markScale`; restore reads `if("markScale" in s) ŌĆ” else if("textScale" in s) ŌĆ”` so any rev-30-era save still loads. (Still sketcher session-UI, not `loadProject` schema ŌĆö tripwire unaffected.)
- **`1├Ś` == original.** Because the base literals are the pre-rev-31 originals and the multiplier defaults to 1, a `1├Ś` plan is byte-equivalent to rev 30's geometry; only `<1├Ś` changes pixels.

**Engine guard CLEAN** ŌĆö all 10 engine/stacking fns extract-and-diff IDENTICAL. The full diff is the `APP_BUILD` bump + the markup/scale lines only. **Verification:** esbuild compile OK; SSR render smoke (group reads "Markup", bare options, default `1├Ś` selected, App mounts); focused export test ŌĆö `Reaction`/`WindLoad` strokes restored to originals at `ts=1` (4.2 / baseline 2 / arrows 1.6) and exactly halved at `ts=0.5` (2.1 / 1 / 0.8), shaft length 21ŌåÆ10.5, and **arrow `<line>` count invariant across scales** (size, not density). Build `APP_BUILD = 113` ("Version 1.13").

**Tweaks if asked:** base sizes live in the `rev 32:`-commented lines (nodes block, `Reaction`, `WindLoad`); a smaller floor or different default is one `<option>` / the `useState(1)` initial; promoting the scale into a shared constant isn't needed since `markScale`/`ts` already is that single factor.

## 4hh. Rev 33 ŌĆö Shear-wall engine extracted to `calcCore.js` (first file split; user-requested)

The user asked to start splitting the monolithic single-file app into modules (motivation: easier debugging + not re-uploading the whole 4k-line file for every change), beginning with the calc engine and doing the rest later. This rev extracts ONLY the shear-wall calculation engine into a new sibling module `src/calcCore.js`. It is a **pure text move ŌĆö zero behavioral change** (proven two ways below). `APP_BUILD` stays **113 ("Version 1.13")**: like the rev-29 Vite scaffold, this is structural/infra, and the user-facing version tracks app-code behavior changes, of which there are none.

- **What moved (verbatim) into `src/calcCore.js`:** the data `SCHEDULE`, `SCHEDULE_STR1`, `schedFor`, `NAIL_EDGE`, `CODES`, `HD_TABLE`; the helpers `isNum`, `xMax`, `numOr0`, `CP`; and the engine fns `calcSegment`, `baseDesignSeg`, `evaluateCandidate`, `generateDesign`. These were lines ~1989ŌĆō2198 of the rev-32 file (the whole block between the "PLYWOOD SHEAR WALL MODULE" banner and the `// ---------- Formatting + dark theme` comment). `calcCore.js` ends with one `export { ŌĆ” }` of all 14 names.
- **Why this block specifically (clean cut, no circular import):** the shear engine is **self-contained** ŌĆö it references only `Math.*` and helpers defined within the block (`schedFor`/`xMax`/`CP`/`HD_TABLE`/`numOr0`/`isNum`). It does NOT use any geometry helper (`keyOf`/`clamp`/`dist`/ŌĆ”) or React. So it can live in its own module with **no imports back into the app file** ŌåÆ no circular dependency. (The wind engine `lineReactions`/`buildSecData`/`findLeewardPartner` is NOT self-contained ŌĆö it uses the geometry helpers that `PlanSketcher` also uses ŌĆö which is exactly why it was left for a later split that also extracts `geometry.js`.)
- **What the app file imports back:** the 10 names actually referenced outside the block ŌĆö `calcSegment, generateDesign, baseDesignSeg, schedFor, HD_TABLE, NAIL_EDGE, CODES, isNum, xMax, numOr0` ŌĆö via `import { ŌĆ” } from "./calcCore.js";` placed immediately after the React import. (`CP`, `evaluateCandidate`, `SCHEDULE`, `SCHEDULE_STR1` have no external callers ŌĆö they stay internal to `calcCore.js` but are still exported for the test harness / future modules.) The "PLYWOOD SHEAR WALL MODULE" banner comment stays in the app file with an added note that the engine now lives in `calcCore.js`.
- **Still in `plan-sketcher-suite.jsx` (deliberately, for the later split):** the wind engine (`lineReactions`/`buildSecData`/`findLeewardPartner`), the design/stacking logic (`lineResults`/`stackSeg`/`stackedLineResults`/`upliftStk`/`withUtil`/`postAllowable`/`hdCapacity`), all React components, `fmt`, the themes/CSS, persistence (`loadProject`/`migrateProject`/`DEFAULT_*`), and `App`. `fmt` calls `isNum` (now imported) ŌĆö fine.
- **Proven byte-identical TWO ways.** (1) **Engine guard:** all **12** guarded fns (`calcSegment`, `generateDesign`, `evaluateCandidate`, `baseDesignSeg`, `lineReactions`, `buildSecData`, `findLeewardPartner`, `lineResults`, `withUtil`, `stackSeg`, `stackedLineResults`, `upliftStk`) extract-and-diff **IDENTICAL** vs the rev-32 baseline ŌĆö the 4 moved ones found in `calcCore.js`, the other 8 in the app file. (2) **Rendered-App diff:** bundled `App` from the rev-32 monolith AND from the post-split pair, `renderToString`'d both ŌåÆ **byte-for-byte identical, 32,000 chars each**. Plus: both files esbuild-compile (the `./calcCore.js` import resolves), comment-balance clean in both, and a direct functional test of `calcCore.js` as an imported module (all 14 exports present; the Structural-I golden `vW = 438.75`; `schedFor("str1")` caps 475/715/930; `schedFor(undefined) === SCHEDULE`).
- **Deploy (IMPORTANT ŌĆö this push ADDS a file).** The repo `src/` now holds **three** source files: `main.jsx` (unchanged ŌĆö still `import App from "./plan-sketcher-suite.jsx"`), `plan-sketcher-suite.jsx` (replaced ŌĆö engine block removed, import added), and **`calcCore.js` (NEW ŌĆö must be created in the repo)**. `index.html`, `package.json`, `vite.config.js`, `.gitignore` are all unchanged (Vite resolves the new relative import automatically; no config needed). So via GitHub web UI: add `src/calcCore.js`, replace `src/plan-sketcher-suite.jsx`, and re-commit this handoff.
- **Preview workflow note (changed by the split).** A multi-file app no longer renders as a standalone Claude artifact (the artifact runtime can't resolve `./calcCore.js`). To keep the ┬¦0 "preview as a live artifact" rule working, **bundle `calcCore.js` + `plan-sketcher-suite.jsx` into one temp single-file jsx and present THAT** (concatenate calcCore minus its `export`, then the app file minus its `calcCore` import ŌĆö or esbuild-bundle). The committed repo stays modular; the preview is a throwaway bundle.
- **Harness impact (see ┬¦6/┬¦6b updates):** the engine byte-identity guard now searches BOTH `calcCore.js` (moved fns) and the app file (the rest), and its extractor handles `const name =` arrows (e.g. `upliftStk`) as well as `function name(`. The golden-suite bundle step now bundles `calcCore.js` directly (it already exports the engine) instead of appending an `export` to a copy of the app file.

## 4ii. Rev 34 ŌĆö Floor diaphragm stops double-counting the roof load (2-story display fix; user-requested)

The user (PE/SE) flagged a load-path error in the section-cut window: in 2-story mode the **2nd-floor diaphragm** line load was shown as `wallRes + wallRes2 + roofLL` ŌĆö i.e. it added the *entire roof diaphragm* (incl. parapets) into the floor diaphragm (e.g. 104 + 104 + 374 = **582 plf**). That is physically wrong. The roof diaphragm does not pour into the floor diaphragm; it dumps into the **2nd-story shear wall**, which transfers down into the **1st-story shear wall as a point load**. The floor diaphragm itself spans only the half-walls directly above and below it. Correct floor diaphragm = `wallRes + wallRes2` = ┬Į┬ĘH┬Ępw + ┬Į┬ĘHŌéé┬Ępw = 104 + 104 = **208 plf**. This is a **display fix only** ŌĆö the reactions/point loads and the stacked overturning/holdown were already correct and must not change.

- **Why the reactions don't move.** The 1st-floor on-plan reaction (11.35k in the user's 60├Ś39 ft, H=HŌéé=13, pw=16 case) was computed from the COMBINED load via `propsForActive`'s `H_eff = H + 2┬ĘHŌéé` (582 plf). That single reaction equals the floor-only diaphragm reaction (208 plf ŌåÆ 4.06k) **plus** the level-2 shear-wall reaction transferred down (374 plf ŌåÆ 7.29k): 4.06 + 7.29 = 11.35k. So lumping it as 582ŌåÆ11.35k vs. stacking 208+roof-via-wall gives the identical total. The fix therefore changes ONLY the displayed line-load label; the combined-load path that produces the point loads is left exactly as-is.
- **`floorDiaphragmPlf` (new helper, next to `propsForActive`).** `useCallback(key => 0.5┬Ę(p.pw)┬Ę((p.H)+(p.HŌéé)))` using `propsFor(key)` (the REAL, un-substituted props). Note the leeward-parapet term and the windward parapet term BOTH cancel out of `combined ŌłÆ roof` (they live only in the roof diaphragm), so the floor diaphragm load is **uniform along a wall** ŌĆö no per-region subdivision, hence one label.
- **`WindLoad` gains `displayPlf` (default null).** When non-null, it renders a SINGLE span `waŌåÆwb` at `displayPlf` instead of the rev-18 per-region coalesced `subLoads`. The plan passes `displayPlf={twoStory && activeFloor===1 ? floorDiaphragmPlf(wl.key) : null}` for both `secH`/`secV` windward walls. So: 1st-floor 2-story view ŌåÆ floor-only label; 2nd-floor view (`displayPlf` null) ŌåÆ roof diaphragm label (374, parapets included) unchanged; 1-story mode (`displayPlf` null) ŌåÆ byte-identical to before.
- **Within-wall dashed divides hidden on the 1st floor.** The `secData.divides` render is gated with `!(twoStory && activeFloor===1)`. Those divides mark where the per-region (combined) plf changes along a wall ŌĆö driven by leeward-parapet variation, which belongs to the ROOF diaphragm. With the floor load uniform, a divide would contradict the single 208 label, so it's suppressed on the 1st floor only (still drawn on the 2nd floor and in 1-story mode). [If the user prefers them kept, un-gate this one render.]
- **`WindWindow` section-cut panel.** `floorLL = wallRes + wallRes2` (dropped `+ roofLL`); the "roof load transferred Ōåō" breakdown `<div>` is removed (the two remaining rows ŌĆö ┬Į┬ĘHŌéé┬Ępw lower-half + ┬Į┬ĘH┬Ępw upper-half ŌĆö now sum to the displayed 208). `SecDiagram2` already takes `floorLL` only for the gold "2nd-flr diaphragm" callout text (the dashed diaphragm LINE is positioned from heights, not the load), so it updates automatically with no geometry change. `roofLL` is unchanged (374) ŌĆö the roof diaphragm is correct as-is.
- **Untouched (verified by reading, not by guard this session ŌĆö user asked not to run tests):** `buildSecData`, `lineReactions`, `findLeewardPartner` (all guarded), `propsForActive` (1st floor still `H_eff = H + 2┬ĘHŌéé`), `secH`/`secV`, `runDesignHandoff`/`forceLbs`, the status-bar base shear, and the entire Design tab + stacking. No guarded engine fn was edited. esbuild compiles both files clean (only the pre-existing duplicate-key warnings in the unused dark `Elevation`). `APP_BUILD = 114` ("Version 1.14").
- **Deploy:** replace `src/plan-sketcher-suite.jsx` ONLY. `calcCore.js`, `main.jsx`, `index.html`, `package.json`, `vite.config.js` are all unchanged.

## 4jj. Rev 35 ŌĆö Mixed-height two-story ┬Ę Step 1/4: one-story wall tagging (user-requested, multi-step)

The user wants to model buildings that are two-story overall but where some walls/portions are only one story (single-story or open-to-above) ŌĆö e.g. the 2-story box inside a 1-story perimeter in the attached schematics. We agreed a full behavior spec and a 4-step build (each step previewed by the user before the next, like the original two-story feature in ┬¦4z). A one-story wall = a diaphragm-connectivity statement: it feeds the **floor** diaphragm (its parapet + top-half + its own roof, which sits at the floor-diaphragm level) and the **foundation**, but never the **roof** diaphragm.

**Step 1 (this rev) is the tag + appearance ONLY ŌĆö no load/analysis change.** With no walls tagged, the app is byte-identical to rev 34. Edits (all in `plan-sketcher-suite.jsx`, none in the guarded engine):
- **State** `const [oneStory,setOneStory]=useState(()=>new Set())` declared next to `noSupport`.
- **Helper** `isOneStory = useCallback(key => twoStory && oneStory.has(key))` next to `isSup`. **Toggle** `toggleOneStory(edge)` next to `toggleSupport`.
- **Menu** new wall-menu button `Ōå¦ Switch to 1-story / Ōåź Switch to 2-story`, gated `{twoStory && (ŌĆ”)}`, between "Takes point load" and "Add node here".
- **Appearance** wall stroke uses `oneSty?C_ONESTORY:C_WALL` with new const `C_ONESTORY="#2E6B4F"` (the design-palette green). The non-load-bearing dashed/dimmed style is applied independently, so a wall that is both reads green + dashed + dimmed.
- **Split migration** `setOneStory(...)` mirrors the `noSupport` line in `splitWall` ŌĆö both halves inherit the tag.
- **Persistence** `oneStory:[...oneStory]` added to the sketcher `get()`; `setOneStory(new Set(s.oneStory||[]))` in `set()` (old files ŌåÆ empty). This is sketcher SESSION-UI, NOT in `loadProject`'s schema, so the schema tripwire is unaffected (same as `noSupport`/`markScale`).
- **Warning** `allOneStory = useMemo(()=> twoStory && graph.edges.length>0 && graph.edges.every(e=>oneStory.has(keyOf(e))))`; renders an amber top-right overlay `ŌÜĀ All walls are 1-story ŌĆö the 2nd floor has no walls` via new `.allonestory-warn` CSS (mirrors `.floorbadge`, sits top-right so it never collides with the top-left floor badge).
- **`APP_BUILD = 115`** ("Version 1.15").

**Engine guard CLEAN** ŌĆö all 12 guarded fns (`findLeewardPartner`/`lineReactions`/`buildSecData`/`lineResults`/`stackSeg`/`stackedLineResults`/`upliftStk`/`withUtil` + `calcSegment`/`generateDesign`/`baseDesignSeg`/`evaluateCandidate`) extract-and-diff identical to the rev-34 baseline. esbuild compile clean (pre-existing dup-key warning in the unused dark `Elevation` only); SSR render smoke PASS (32,149 chars).

**Confirmed spec (locked before coding) ŌĆö drives Steps 2ŌĆō4:**
- **Step 2 ŌĆö 2nd-floor (roof) exclusion.** On the 2nd-floor view only two-story walls exist. Implement by handing `buildSecData` a FILTERED graph = the full graph minus one-story walls (+ their orphaned nodes) and a recomputed `loop`; the full graph still RENDERS all walls (green ones drawn, load-less). This drops 1-story walls from windward collection, the `overlapShadow` test, AND `lineReactions` supports in one move ŌĆö engine untouched. (NB: zeroing via `propsFor` is NOT enough ŌĆö a 1-story wall geometrically in front of the box would wrongly *shadow* the box; removing it from the graph is the fix.)
- **Step 3 ŌĆö 1st-floor accumulation (the 454).** A windward wall's floor-diaphragm plf VARIES along its length: at each across-wind station it sums the connected strips in its downwind shadow ŌĆö its own ┬Į┬ĘH┬Ępw (+ its parapet if it is 1-story, whose roof is at the floor level) + the **bottom half of any two-story wall behind it (┬Į┬ĘHŌéé┬Ępw, one face)** + leeward parapet. So the front wall splits into regions (e.g. 454 where the box is behind it, 374 where it isn't). The app ALREADY walks back-walls + subdivides the windward span for the leeward parapet (`backs`/breakpoints/`subLoads` in `buildSecData`); Step 3 is a NEW wind fn that extends that pattern to also add the back two-story wall's ┬Į┬ĘHŌéé, then reuses `lineReactions` for the point loads ŌĆö guarded `buildSecData` stays byte-identical. Worked example from the user's schematic: `32├Ś5 + 16├Ś13/2 + 22├Ś5 (=374, the front 1-story wall) + 16├Ś10/2 (=80, the box behind) = 454`.
- **Step 4 ŌĆö section cuts + design handoff + finalize.** A 1-story wall cuts as a SINGLE-story elevation (route to `SecDiagram`, or `SecDiagram2` with HŌéé=0); asymmetric cut (1-story front / 2-story back) draws front at its own height, leeward height/parapet from the back wall. Handoff: `buildFloor(2)` on the filtered graph, `buildFloor(1)` with accumulation; a 1-story floor-1 line has no aligned floor-2 partner so it stays UNSTACKED automatically (existing `stackedLineResults`). Also revisit the rev-34 floor-1 `divides` hide so it suppresses only on two-story walls (1-story walls vary along their length and should show divides).
- **Other confirmed details:** accumulation amount = ┬Į┬ĘHŌéé┬Ępw, one face (Ō£ģ user). One-story parapets ŌåÆ floor diaphragm; two-story parapets ŌåÆ roof diaphragm (Ō£ģ). Two-story region assumed to CLOSE into a loop ŌĆö exact for a freestanding/convex box; an open set falls back to the centroid-normal heuristic ŌĆö acceptable for v1 (Ō£ģ). The all-1-story warning is the agreed degenerate handling (Ō£ģ). rev-34's floor-only display stays valid: it was the UNIFORM two-story special case where the only parapet is at the roof, so nothing connects a parapet to the floor diaphragm; the mixed case legitimately gains floor-level parapet terms.

**Deploy:** replace `src/plan-sketcher-suite.jsx` ONLY ŌĆö `calcCore.js`, `main.jsx`, `index.html`, `package.json`, `vite.config.js` all UNCHANGED.

## 4kk. Rev 36 ŌĆö Mixed-height two-story ┬Ę Step 2/4: 2nd-floor (roof diaphragm) excludes 1-story walls

Step 2 makes the tag *do* something. On the 2nd-floor view (and the floor-2 design lines), a 1-story wall no longer participates in the roof diaphragm ŌĆö it collects no line load, casts no overlap-shadow, and takes no point-load reaction. Only the two-story walls carry the roof. The 1st-floor view and 1-story mode are unchanged (floor-1 effects are Step 3). Matches the user's "2ND FLOOR PLAN" schematic (loads + reactions only on the 2-story box).

- **`twoStoryGraph` (new memo).** `if(!twoStory || oneStory.size===0) return graph;` else `{ edges: graph.edges.filter(e=>!oneStory.has(keyOf(e))), nodes: graph.nodes.filter(used) }` where `used` = node ids still referenced by the kept edges. So an untagged building returns the SAME `graph` reference ŌåÆ byte-identical downstream.
- **`twoStoryLoop` (new memo).** `loopInfo(twoStoryGraph.nodes, twoStoryGraph.edges)`. NB: a perimeter+box footprint is TWO rings, so the full-graph `loop` is already `null` (loopInfo wants one cycle covering all nodes) and `buildSecData` uses its centroid-normal fallback; but the filtered two-story graph is just the box = ONE ring ŌåÆ `twoStoryLoop` is non-null ŌåÆ exact exterior normals for the box.
- **Live render.** `const roofView = twoStory && activeFloor===2; secGraph = roofView?twoStoryGraph:graph; secLoop = roofView?twoStoryLoop:loop;` then `secH`/`secV` call `buildSecData(sections.*, secGraph, secLoop, isSup, propsForActive)` (deps swapped graph/loop ŌåÆ secGraph/secLoop). Both are stable references (one of two memoized/state objects), so no extra recompute. Walls still all RENDER off the full `graph` ŌĆö green 1-story walls are drawn, just load-less on floor 2.
- **Design handoff.** `buildFloor(floor)` gained `fg/fl` locals (`= twoStory&&floor===2 ? twoStoryGraph/twoStoryLoop : graph/loop`) used in its two `buildSecData` calls, the reactionŌåÆedge lookup (`fg.edges.find`), the node lookups (`fg.nodes.find`), and the support-extent scan (`fg.edges.forEach`). `runDesignHandoff` deps gained `twoStoryGraph`, `twoStoryLoop`.
- **Why filter the graph instead of zeroing props:** the guarded `buildSecData` runs an `overlapShadow` test that drops a windward wall when another windward wall sits in front of it. A 1-story wall geometrically in FRONT of the box (e.g. the perimeter) would wrongly *shadow* the box's windward wall if it stayed in the graph with zero load. Removing it from the graph excludes it from windward collection, the shadow test, AND `lineReactions` supports in one move ŌĆö and the guarded engine is never edited.

**Engine guard CLEAN** (all 12 fns identical to the rev-34 baseline). esbuild compile clean; SSR render smoke PASS (32,149 chars). New checked-in **`work/test_step2.cjs`** (6 asserts through the REAL bundled engine on a perimeter-1-story + box-2-story fixture: full graph loads some perimeter wall; FILTERED graph loads no perimeter wall, still loads a box wall, confines reactions to box walls, and yields a base shear that is `>0` but `<` the full-graph base shear). `APP_BUILD = 116` ("Version 1.16").

**Still to do:** Step 3 (1st-floor 454 accumulation ŌĆö a NEW wind fn that extends the back-wall subdivision pattern to add the back two-story wall's ┬Į┬ĘHŌéé┬Ępw, reusing `lineReactions`; also revisit the rev-34 floor-1 `divides` hide so it suppresses only on two-story walls) ┬Ę Step 4 (1-story section cut = single-story elevation; asymmetric cut; design-handoff finalize incl. 1-story floor-1 lines staying unstacked).

## 4ll. Rev 37 ŌĆö Mixed-height two-story ┬Ę Step 3/4: 1st-floor (floor diaphragm) accumulation ŌĆö "the 454"

The 1st-floor view + floor-1 design now show the mixed building's true floor-diaphragm demand. A windward wall's plf varies along its length, summing the strips connected to the floor diaphragm in its downwind shadow. Worked example (user's schematic): a 1-story perimeter front wall reads `32├Ś5 + 16├Ś13/2 + 22├Ś5 = 374` where nothing two-story stands behind it, and `+ 16├Ś10/2 = 454` over the stretch where the 2-story box does ŌĆö split by a dashed tributary divide.

- **`buildSecDataF1(section, graph, loop, isSup, propsFor, isOne)` (new module fn, after `buildSecData`).** A focused copy of `buildSecData`: identical windward determination, `overlapShadow`, line-grouping, back-wall `backs` gathering + breakpoint subdivision, `divides`, and reaction aggregation; calls `findLeewardPartner` and `lineReactions` verbatim. Only the per-wall / per-sub-region load rule differs. `isOne(key)` = the wall is tagged 1-story. **Pass it the RAW `propsFor` (mergeWallProps), NOT `propsForActive`** ŌĆö the fn applies the floor-diaphragm formula itself.
- **Load rule.** `baseOf(key)` = ┬Į┬ĘH┬Ępw + (1-story ? par┬ĘqWind : ┬Į┬ĘHŌéé┬Ępw). For each windward sub-region: `plf = base + leePar┬ĘqLee + acc`, where `leePar` = farthest-downwind back wall's parapet but only counted if THAT back wall `isOne` (a 2-story back wall's parapet is at the roof, not the floor), and `acc` = ┬Į┬ĘHŌéé┬Ępw of the NEAREST 2-story back wall covering the sub-region (one face). `backs[]` now carries `{lo,hi,d, par:(one?bp.par:0), h2:(one?0:┬Į┬ĘHŌéé┬Ępw)}`; the box's lo/hi become breakpoints, so the front wall splits into 374/454.
- **Wiring.** `mixed1 = twoStory && activeFloor===1 && oneStory.size>0`. `secH`/`secV` use `buildSecDataF1(ŌĆ”graph,loopŌĆ”propsFor,isOneStory)` when `mixed1`, else `buildSecData(ŌĆ”secGraph,secLoopŌĆ”propsForActive)` (deps add `mixed1,propsFor,isOneStory`). `buildFloor(1)` mirrors it via local `mixedF1`. The rev-34 floor-1 `displayPlf` override and the `divides` hide are both re-gated `ŌĆ”activeFloor===1 && !mixed1`, so the mixed wall shows its real per-region labels + divides, and uniform 2-story (no tags) is byte-identical to rev 36.
- **Self-consistency.** A 2-story windward wall's `base` = ┬Į┬ĘH┬Ępw + ┬Į┬ĘHŌéé┬Ępw = `floorDiaphragmPlf` (the rev-34 floor-only value), so the two models agree where they overlap. The box's near face is shadowed-and-dropped from its own windward line by `overlapShadow`; its floor contribution is RECOVERED onto the front wall via `acc` (no double count). The roof half of the box still goes to floor-2 / stacks down separately (Step 2 + existing stacking).

**Engine guard CLEAN** (12/12 identical to the rev-34 baseline). esbuild compile clean; SSR render smoke PASS (32,149); Step-2 regression PASS. New checked-in **`work/test_step3.cjs`** (real `buildSecDataF1` on a 1-story-perimeter 40├Ś30 + 2-story-box x:10ŌĆō30/y:9ŌĆō21 fixture, NŌĆōS wind): asserts the windward bottom wall's sub-region plfs are `[374,374,454]`, the highŌłÆlow difference is exactly ┬Į┬ĘHŌéé┬Ępw = 80, the middle third (over the box) carries 454, the box walls are absent from `windLoads` (shadowed ŌåÆ accumulated), and a divide is emitted. `APP_BUILD = 117` ("Version 1.17").

**Still to do ŌĆö Step 4 (final):** section cuts (a 1-story wall cuts as a SINGLE-story elevation ŌĆö route to `SecDiagram`, or `SecDiagram2` with HŌéé=0; asymmetric 1-story-front / 2-story-back draws front at its own height with leeward read from the back wall); design-handoff finalize (confirm 1-story floor-1 lines stay UNSTACKED ŌĆö they have no aligned floor-2 partner, so `stackedLineResults` already leaves them alone). Then full mixed-height sign-off.

## 4oo. Rev 40 ŌĆö Mixed-height two-story ┬Ę sequence-based overall section cut (A/B/C/C-reverse)

The section-cut window is now a true overall-building section, driven by the ordered run of walls the cut crosses. Resolves the two issues the user raised on rev 39 (the section changed between floors; Section C drew like Section A) and renders all four schematic section types.

- **Section type = wall sequence.** `sectionSequence(sAcross, axis, sign, graph, propsFor, isOne)` (module fn after `nearestTwoStoryBehind`) returns every `recv`-orientation wall whose across-wind span includes the cut position `sAcross`, ordered by downwind depth (windwardŌåÆleeward): `[{key, one, H, H2, par, pw, qWind, qLee, depth}]`. The 1/2-story pattern is the type: `1┬Ę2┬Ę2┬Ę1`=A, `1┬Ę1`=B, `1┬Ę2┬Ę2`=C, `2┬Ę2┬Ę1`=C-reverse. Always the full graph ŌåÆ floor-independent.
- **Floor independence.** The open-section `useEffect` now computes `seq` from `po.sAcross` on the full graph and anchors `activeWall.key = seq[0].key` (the true windward wall) rather than the floor-filtered `sc.windLoads[0]`. `activeSection.seq` is recomputed from `activeWall.sAcross` (fallback: the active wall's center).
- **`SecDiagramSeq`** (replaced `SecDiagramMix`). Draws N walls frontŌåÆback at their own story heights; floor diaphragm dashed across all at the 1-story top; roof diaphragm over the contiguous 2-story block (`twoIdx`); windward pressure on the front wall (full height + parapet), leeward on the back; front & back editable through the live `v`/`upd` buffer (front gets an HŌéé box when it is 2-story, for C-reverse), interior walls display-only. No per-type branching ŌĆö the sequence is the input.
- **`WindWindow` routing.** `seq = section.seq||[]`; `hasOne/hasTwo`; `mixedSeq = twoStory && hasOne && hasTwo && seq.length>=2`. `mixedSeq ? <SecDiagramSeq seq floorLL={floorLLmix}> : twoStoryView ? <SecDiagram2> : <SecDiagram>`. `floorLLmix = seqBase + seqLeePar + seqAcc` with `seqBase = ┬Į┬ĘH┬Ępw + (front 1-story ? windPar : 0)`, `seqAcc = front 1-story ? ┬Į┬ĘHŌéé┬Ępw of the nearest 2-story in the sequence : ┬Į┬ĘHŌéé┬Ępw of the front wall`, `seqLeePar` only if the back wall is 1-story ŌĆö matching `buildSecDataF1`. Breakdown shows ┬Į┬ĘH┬Ępw + parapets + the poured-forward ┬Į┬ĘHŌéé┬Ępw (478 at HŌéé=13).

`SecDiagram`/`SecDiagram2`/the guarded engine untouched. Engine guard CLEAN (12/12); compile clean; render smoke PASS. New **`work/test_step5.cjs`** PASSES (AŌåÆ[1,2,2,1], BŌåÆ[1,1], CŌåÆ[1,2,2], C-revŌåÆ[2,2,1]; floor-independent; `SecDiagramSeq` draws 2+2 / 1+2 markers; C-reverse front designs a 2-story wall). `test_step4b.cjs` retired (asserted on the removed `SecDiagramMix`). Steps 2/3/4 regressions pass. `APP_BUILD = 120` ("Version 1.20").

**Pending the user's eyeball:** wall spacing, proportions, labels, and which props are editable are a first pass ŌĆö all inside `SecDiagramSeq`. Also note `nearestTwoStoryBehind` (rev 39) is still defined and used by `activeSection.behind`, but `behind` is now superseded by `seq` for the drawing/load; it can be removed in a later cleanup if desired.

## 4pp. Rev 41 ŌĆö Mixed-height two-story ┬Ę section cut draws the Level-2 (roof) pressures + value; diaphragms renamed Level 1 / Level 2

Three display-only fixes to `SecDiagramSeq` (the mixed overall-building section cut), driven by the user comparing it to the CAD schematic (SECTION A / SECTION C). The guarded engine and every load value are byte-identical.

- **Block pressures drawn (the missing roof-diaphragm source).** rev 40's `SecDiagramSeq` drew windward pressure only on the sequence FRONT wall and leeward parapet only on the sequence BACK wall; the 2-story block in the middle drew as bare lines ŌĆö so the pressures that produce the upper diaphragm had no visible source. New draw group: front-most 2-story wall `bw=twoIdx[0]` gets WINDWARD `pw` arrows over its UPPER story (`topY(fw)`ŌåÆits own floor line; the lower story is shadowed by whatever stands in front) + `qWind` arrows over its parapet; back-most 2-story wall `bl=twoIdx[last]` gets its LEEWARD parapet `qLee` (arrows to the right). Gated `bw!==0` / `bl!==last` so a block end that coincides with the sequence front/back (Section C / C-reverse, already drawn by the front-windward / back-leeward code) isn't drawn twice. Block parapet pressures read `seq[bw].qWind` / `seq[bl].qLee` (the back-block leeward pressure is NOT `W[bl].q`, which is the interior wall's `qWind`). Arrow lengths via a new `aOf(psf)=psf>0?max(psf┬ĘaS,6):0`; `maxPsf` (the arrow scale) now spans every wall's `pw/qWind/qLee` so block arrows stay proportional and within the 30px budget.
- **Level-2 (roof) value shown.** `WindWindow` computes `roofLLseq` from the block's front/back `seq` walls: `twoIxSeq = seq indices of !one walls`, `bf=twoIxSeq[0]`, `bb=twoIxSeq[last]`; `roofLLseq = ┬Į┬ĘblkH2┬ĘblkPw + blkWPar + blkLPar`, where `blkH2/blkPw` come from the front block wall, `blkWPar = front.par┬Ęfront.qWind`, `blkLPar = back.par┬Ęback.qLee` ŌĆö and where a block end equals the editable sequence front (`bf===0`) / back (`bb===seq.length-1`) the live `v` values (`v.H2/v.pw/v.wH┬Ęv.wQ` / `v.lH┬Ęv.lQ`) substitute, so Section C / C-reverse edits flow through. Same SHAPE as the uniform-two-story `roofLL = ┬Į┬ĘHŌéé┬Ępw + windPar + leePar`. Passed to `SecDiagramSeq` as a `roofLL` prop, rendered in the upper callout (replacing "ŌåÆ block's own walls"), and added to the breakdown panel as a "Level 2 diaphragm line load ŌåÆ designs the level-2 (2-story block) walls" section with `┬Į┬ĘHŌéé┬Ępw (block, upper ┬Į)` + `windward + leeward parapet (block)` sub-rows (gated `roofLLseq>0`). Schematic case 10ft/16psf + 6ft┬Ę(32+22): `┬Į┬Ę10┬Ę16 + 6┬Ę32 + 6┬Ę22 = 404 plf`.
- **Rename ŌåÆ Level 1 / Level 2 (and the naming implication).** Every user-facing "roof diaphragm" ŌåÆ **"Level 2 diaphragm"**, "floor"/"2nd-flr"/"2nd-floor diaphragm" ŌåÆ **"Level 1 diaphragm"**, across `SecDiagramSeq`, `SecDiagram2`, and both `WindWindow` breakdown panels; the "designs Nth-floor shear walls" sublabels ŌåÆ "designs the level-N (upper/lower) shear walls". The mapping is unambiguous because two conventions agree: name-by-the-story-it-designs (roof designs the level-2/upper walls; floor designs the level-1/lower walls) AND name-by-elevation (the lower/first diaphragm = Level 1, the upper/second = Level 2) both give **roof = Level 2, floor = Level 1**. The rename is confined to displayed strings + the comments at the label sites. The `roofLL` / `floorLL` / `roofLLseq` / `floorLLmix` VARIABLE names are intentionally KEPT (a mapping comment was added at their definitions) ŌĆö renaming identifiers would be pure churn next to the guarded-engine-adjacent UI and buys nothing functional. **No value, engine, reaction, load-path, or design-handoff change** ŌĆö purely the labels a user reads.
- **Overlap fix.** The rev-40 callout sat at `calloutX=VBW-84=278` while the leeward wall was at `rightX=284`, so the "ŌĆ” diaphragm ŌĆ” plf" text overlapped the wall line (visible in the user's screenshots). Fixed by widening `VBW 362ŌåÆ380`, pulling the wall span left (`rightX 284ŌåÆ250`), and moving the callouts to `calloutX=300` ŌĆö clear of the wall (250) and its leeward arrows (Ōēż30 ŌåÆ 280).

`SecDiagram`/`SecDiagram2` geometry and the guarded wind + shear-wall engines untouched. Engine guard CLEAN (12/12 byte-identical); modular compile clean; render smoke PASS (modular render ŌēĪ inlined preview). NEW focused SSR render test (Section A 1┬Ę2┬Ę2┬Ę1, in `work/_rev41_focus.cjs` against an exports-augmented copy): "Level 1 diaphragm" + "Level 2 diaphragm" present, zero legacy "Roof/Floor/2nd-floor diaphragm" strings, Level-2 value `404` rendered, block pressure arrows drawn (26 `dArrM` lines vs the pre-block count), and `calloutX(300) > rightX(250)+arrows(280)`. Steps 2/3/4/5 regressions + engine guard pass. `APP_BUILD = 121` ("Version 1.21").

**Known limitation (RESOLVED in rev 42 ŌĆö see ┬¦4qq):** rev 41 read the block's PLAN props and the interior block walls were display-only. rev 42 makes every wall in the section cut editable (height + pressure), so an interior block wall can now be changed directly and the Level-2 value/arrows follow.

## 4qq. Rev 42 ŌĆö Mixed-height two-story ┬Ę interior block walls fully editable (height + pressure)

Removes the rev-41 limitation. In `SecDiagramSeq` the 2-story block walls sitting between the sequence front/back were display-only; now every wall the cut crosses is as editable as the front/back. The block FRONT wall (windward face) exposes `pw` ┬Ę `H` ┬Ę `HŌéé` ┬Ę `par` ┬Ę `qWind`; the block BACK wall (leeward face) exposes `qLee` ┬Ę `par` ┬Ę `H` ┬Ę `HŌéé`. Display/UI only ŌĆö the guarded engine and all formulas are byte-identical.

- **`setVals` (parent) takes an explicit key.** It already resolved `"self"` ŌåÆ active wall and `"lee"` ŌåÆ leeward partner; added `else if(target && target!=="self") key=target` so any edge key edits that wall's `wallProps` entry. Backward-compatible (real keys from `keyOf` never equal `"self"`/`"lee"`).
- **`WindWindow` ŌåÆ `SecDiagramSeq`** passes `commit={(key,prop,val)=>setVals(key,{[prop]:val})}`. Front/back keep the `v`/`upd` path.
- **`SecDiagramSeq` made key-aware.** New `commit` prop; a raw-string buffer `ebuf` keyed `"${key}:${prop}"` so a partially-typed "13." isn't collapsed; `open(field,prop,cx,cy,key)` carries an optional key and `Box` forwards `wkey`; `seqVal(key,prop)` reads the live value; and a new editable-box group on the interior block ends, gated `bw!==0`/`bl!==last` so a block end that IS the sequence front/back keeps its original boxes (no duplicate). The floating input branches on `edit.key`: keyed ŌåÆ value `ebuf ?? String(seqVal)`, `onChange` ŌåÆ `setEbuf` + `commit(key,prop,num)`, `onBlur` clears the buffer entry; unkeyed ŌåÆ the existing `v`/`upd` path. Enter/Escape blur (runs the keyed cleanup).
- **Live with no extra wiring.** A keyed edit writes `wallProps[key]`; `propsFor` and thus `activeSection.seq`/`section.seq` recompute every render, and `roofLLseq` (Level-2 value), the floor accumulation `seqAcc` (Level-1), and `propOf(interior)` (the drawing) all already read from `seq`. So a block-wall height/pressure edit flows straight into the values and arrows ŌĆö identical behavior to a front/back edit, which goes through `v` and also writes `wallProps`.

`SecDiagram`/`SecDiagram2` and the guarded engines untouched. Engine guard CLEAN (12/12 byte-identical); compile clean; render smoke PASS (modular ŌēĪ inlined preview). The rev-41 behaviour test still passes 8/8 (rename + Level-2 value 404 + 26 arrows). NEW **`work/_rev42_edit.cjs`** (jsdom) PASSES 8/8: mounts `SecDiagramSeq` on Section A (1┬Ę2┬Ę2┬Ę1, keys W0/BF/BB/W3), clicks all 15 editable boxes, asserts the 9 interior boxes route to `commit` with interior keys BF & BB across `pw/H/HŌéé/par/qWind/qLee` at numeric values while the 6 front/back boxes still route to `upd` (W0/W3 never committed).
